name: Ranni the Witch | Elden Ring Wiki
Ranni the Witchis anNPCinElden Ring.Ranni the Witchis a mysterious figure who first introduces herself asRenna. Upon meeting her again atThree Sisters, she reveals her true name and eventually will recruit you into her servitude, sending you off in search of a hidden treasure. This page covers vital information for Ranni's questline forElden Ring.
I am the witch Ranni. I stole Death long ago, and search now for the dark path.
Ranni is the daughter ofRadagonandRennala, as such she is a princess of theCarian Royal Family. After Radagon departed and became the consort toQueen Marika, Ranni and her siblings were raised todemigodstatus, as they were now the children of the consort of a goddess. Unlike her siblings however, she was identified as a potential successor to Queen Marika by the Two Fingers, and her status was further elevated to that of anEmpyrean, and like Marika, granted her own shadow,Blaidd.
She appears to have some involvement in The Night of Black Knives, where Black Knife Assassins stole a shard of the Rune of Death and murderedGodwyn, the Golden. At the same time, Ranni seems to have lost her original body and now resides as a spirit inhabiting an artificial doll body. She now seeks a long-lost treasure with the aid of her loyal followers,War Counselor Iji,Preceptor Seluvis, her shadowBlaidd, and the Tarnished if they choose.
Ranni the Witch can be found atRanni's Risein theThree Sisterssub-region ofLiurnia of the Lakesfor a majority of  Ranni's questline.
Ranni is first encountered going by the nameRennawhen the player teleports or rests at theChurch of EllehSite of Grace, after you have metMelinaand acquiredTorrent.
Once she has arrived, she will call out to the player to approach and speak with them. Upon doing so and answering her question in the affirmative, she will gift the player with theSpirit Calling Belland theLone Wolf Ashes. She will then disappear after being spoken to again, walking far enough away from her, or attempting to rest at the Site of Grace. [Map Link]
If the player somehow misses their first encounter with Ranni, this will not prevent her quest from being completed. She can next be found in theLiurniaregion, at the top ofRanni's Rise. To access the area where Ranni's Rise resides, you must defeatRoyal Knight Lorettaat theCaria Manor.
If her initial encounter is missed wherein the player receives theSpirit Calling BellandLone Wolf Ashesfrom Ranni, both can then be found and purchased from theTwin Maiden Husksat theRoundtable Hold.
NOTE: Ranni will not appear in Ranni's Rise for the next step of her quest line if the Radahn Festival has already started atRedmane Castle(the Radahn Festival begins outside of Ranni's quest line progression if you have either activated theGrand Lift of Dectusor activated any Sites of Grace found within theAltus Plateau). This is becauseBlaiddis required to continue her quest line, and he will not leave the Radahn Festival untilStarscourge Radahnhas been defeated. Once Starscourge Radahn has been defeated, Ranni will reappear at Ranni's Rise and her quest line can be continued from then on.
Ranni is later found inLiurniaatopRanni's Rise. She tasks the player with finding the hidden treasure ofNokronand asks that you speak with three people in her service:War Counselor Iji, Half-Wolf WarriorBlaidd, and PreceptorSeluvis. The three will then appear as spectral projections within her tower that can be spoken with.The player will be unable to leave the tower area until all three people have been spoken with and their dialogue exhausted (a fog wall barrier will physically block the player from leaving the area by foot/hoof and fast travel will be disabled). After speaking to the three, returning to Ranni and speaking with her will have her reveal that she is going to fall into a deep slumber soon and will not be able to speak with the player for some time. Once the player is finished speaking with Ranni, the player will be able to leave the area and fast travel again as normal.Upon first meeting her at Ranni's Rise, if she tells you to begone after mentioning the curse mark on her discarded body and won't recruit you into her service, you will need to return toRogierat theRoundtable Holdand speak with him. He will suggest that you join into her service in order to learn more about where her curse mark could be found. You can then return to Ranni and speak with her to continue her quest line.
The player will be unable to leave the tower area until all three people have been spoken with and their dialogue exhausted (a fog wall barrier will physically block the player from leaving the area by foot/hoof and fast travel will be disabled). After speaking to the three, returning to Ranni and speaking with her will have her reveal that she is going to fall into a deep slumber soon and will not be able to speak with the player for some time. Once the player is finished speaking with Ranni, the player will be able to leave the area and fast travel again as normal.
Upon first meeting her at Ranni's Rise, if she tells you to begone after mentioning the curse mark on her discarded body and won't recruit you into her service, you will need to return toRogierat theRoundtable Holdand speak with him. He will suggest that you join into her service in order to learn more about where her curse mark could be found. You can then return to Ranni and speak with her to continue her quest line.
Blaidd will be waiting in theSiofra Riverarea [Map Link] (travel east from the Siofra River Bank Site of Grace until you reach the area where a Spirit Spring can be found, Blaidd will be standing nearby. However, be sure to defeat any enemies nearby as they can pursue you and cause issues with speaking with Blaidd). He will reveal that he suspects thatPreceptor Seluvisknows more than he lets on and suggests that you go and speak with him. Upon speaking with Seluvis, he will inform you thatSorceress Sellenmight have some information as to how to enter Nokron, and then provides you withSeluvis's Introductionto show her. Upon speaking with Sellen at the Waypoint Ruins [Map Link] and showing her Seluvis's Introduction, she informs the player thatStarscourge Radahnhas used his power to stop the movement of the stars, and that the only way to restore their movement and find an entrance into Nokron is to slay him.NOTE: Informing Blaidd of what you've learned from Sellen concerning the stars and Radahn's actions will trigger the festival and temporarily alter the accessible layout ofRedmane Castle, also potentially pausing certain NPC quests and interactions. Moreso, there have been cases where only talking to Sellen without talking to Blaidd afterwards also causes the festival to trigger.Please note, if the player was unable to tolerate his "pleasant demeanor" and has killed Preceptor Seluvis, Blaidd will be hostile to you, and cause Ranni's quest line to halt until the player seeks Absolution at the Church of Vows.Alternative ways to trigger the festival (and thus to kill Starscourge Radahn) are:Accessing Altus Plateau, either via activating the Grand Lift of Dectus or through the Ruin-Strewn Precipice, will automatically trigger the festival on Redmane Castle.The player can also accessRedmane Castleearlier, talk toJerrenand tell him aboutIji, which in turn will suggest you tell something to Iji. If the player then goes back to Iji and talks to him about Jerren, he will tell the player about going back to the festival, thus activating it. This can be done even if the player hasn't met Blaidd at Siofra River.

The player can also accessRedmane Castleearlier, talk toJerrenand tell him aboutIji, which in turn will suggest you tell something to Iji. If the player then goes back to Iji and talks to him about Jerren, he will tell the player about going back to the festival, thus activating it. This can be done even if the player hasn't met Blaidd at Siofra River.
Once Radahn has been slain, the stars will be freed to continue their flight, with one of them landing somewhere nearby. Returning to Iji and speaking with him reveals that the fallen star struckLimgrave(the site is south ofMistwood, fairly close to the ruins where the player could have first met Blaidd) and has created a new entrance into Nokron. Travelling to Limgrave, the landing site is hard to miss, as gravity magic from the fallen star has caused large chunks of rock to become permanently suspended in the air above the landing site. By carefully making their way down, the player can reach the city of Nokron. To reach the section of the city that holds the treasure Ranni wants, you must push through until you reach the Ancestral Woods Site of Grace [Map Link] and then jump across the nearby ledge and back into the city. Continue onward into the city and you will eventually find a treasure chest containing theFingerslayer Blade, the secret treasure of Nokron that Ranni seeks.
NOTE:Giving Ranni the Fingerslayer Blade will causePreceptor Seluvisto become a lifeless puppet, which effectively locks you out of further interaction in his questline (And possibly prevents you from giving Seluvis' Potion toDung Eater). If you want to get theMagic Scorpion Charmfrom Seluvis in this playthrough, you need to start and/or continue through his quest line until he gifts the amulet to you, before giving Ranni the Fingerslayer Blade. After receiving the Magic Scorpion Charm, you may safely carry on with Ranni's quest line.If Seluvis has given you theAmber Draughtto give to Ranni at this point, once you have given her the Fingerslayer Blade you will no longer have the option to give the Amber Draught to Ranni.However, don't be afraid of losing the option to give her the Amber Draught; As you aren't rewarded with anything for trying to give it to her, because it doesn't work on her and only serves to make her disappointed with you and halt her quest line until you seek Absolution at theChurch of Vows.

Upon returning to Ranni and giving her the Fingerslayer Blade, she will reward the player with theCarian Inverted Statue, which they can use at the pedestal at the entrance to theCarian Study Hallto reach the top of the Divine Tower of Liurnia. After speaking with her, Ranni will leave to continue her quest alone. Upon arriving at the top of theDivine Tower of Liurnia, you will be able to find theCursemark of Deathupon the remains of Ranni's original body, which is severely burnt.
After giving the Fingerslayer Blade to Ranni, you can speak with Iji, and he will tell you where Ranni has gone (mentioning Renna's Rise in the process) and theCarian Filigreed Crestwill be added to his merchant inventory for purchase, if you had yet to unlock its availability.
At this point, the seal blocking access toRenna's Risewill have vanished, allowing access inside the tower. Upon reaching the top of the ladder within, you can find a chest containing theSnow Witch Setthat Ranni wore. Upon reaching the top of the tower, you can find awaygatethat will transport you toAinsel River Main, where you can loot aMiniature Rannidoll nearby. After acquiring the doll, rest at the Ainsel River Main Site of Grace. [Map Link] You will see a new option listed amongst the others, that being "Talk to miniature Ranni." Select this option three times and Ranni will speak to you revealing that Ranni has possessed the doll. Annoyed at your interference, she will then task the player with defeating theBaleful Shadowfound further into the area. The Baleful Shadow can be found just beyond theNokstella Waterfall BasinSite of Grace inNokstella, Eternal City. It is an agile and fairly strong opponent, so take caution when fighting it. After defeating the Baleful Shadow, Ranni will thank the player and reward them with theDiscarded Palace Key. Ranni will then say farewell as she still has things to do, her spirit leaving the doll.
You are able to use the Discarded Palace Key to unlock the chest found in theRaya LucariaGrand Library next toRennala. Inside you will find theDark Moon Ring. Once you have acquired the ring, travel back to theLake of Rotin theAinsel Riverarea, and continue onward into theGrand Cloister.
By interacting with the stone coffin in theGrand Cloister[Map Link] (you can interact with it from a distance so that you do not have to stand in the Scarlet Rot water), the player can access a new area where they can find and defeatAstel, Naturalborn of the Void. After its defeat, a new exit path can be traversed through (without having the Dark Moon Ring, an impassable magic seal blocks this exit). This path allows access to the southern-most section of Liurnia, theMoonlight Altar. Your next destination is the nearbyCathedral of Manus Celes. After collecting the 9Starlight Shardsinside scattered about and 1 outside near the stone object on the north side, drop down the hole near the Site of Grace and continue through the tunnel until you reach a recent battle site.Please note,Glintstone Dragon Adulawill suddenly materialize near theCathedral of Manus Celes, regardless of whether or not the dragon was forced to retreat atThree Sisters, so take caution when exploring the area.

Interact with Ranni's doll body to place the Dark Moon Ring on Ranni's finger. Her doll body will then disappear and Ranni, fully restored to her previous life-sized doll form, will appear and thank the player. She confirms that the player is now her consort and promises that they will meet again. After Ranni vanishes, an item will appear where she once stood. Loot the item to acquire theDark Moon Greatsword.
Provided Ranni's quest line has been completed; after defeating the Elden Beast, a blue summon sign will appear on the ground near Marika's broken remains. The player can interact with this summon sign (instead of interacting with Marika's remains) to acquire the"Age of the Stars" ending. Doing so will also unlock a related game achievement/trophy.
I am the witch Ranni. I stole Death long ago, and search now for the dark path. That I might one day upend the whole of it, and rid the world of all that came before.
Ranni the Witch, also known asLunar Princess Ranni, is acharacterinELDEN RING(2022). She is one of theDemigods, and the focus of one of the game's most elaborate questlines.
Originally known asLunar Princess Ranni, she was the daughter ofRadagon, a champion of theGolden Order, andQueen Rennala, head of both theCarian Royal Familyand theAcademy of Raya Lucaria. She had two older brothers,RadahnandRykard.[1]
Ranni was also anEmpyrean, meaning she had the potential to one day succeedQueen Marikaas the divine ruler of theLands Between.[2]TheTwo Fingerschose her as a potential successor and granted her aShadowby the name ofBlaiddto be her vassal.[3]He was approved of by Rennala, and was raised as her foster brother. Ranni grew up playing with Blaidd, and they were often accompanied byIji, atrollblacksmith who served the Carian royals.[4]
Led by the hand of her mother Rennala, young Ranni would encounter herDark Moon. What she beheld was cold, dark and veiled in occult mystery.[5]Deep in the woods, she would also encounter a snowy crone, known simply as the "Snow Witch", who would go on to become her secret mentor.[6]She was an old witch well versed in cold-based sorceries, and she taught Ranni to fear the dark moon as she imparted her magic.[7][8]The full Dark Moon, cold and leaden, would become Ranni's sigil and symbol of her power and authority.[9][10]
At some point, Ranni's father would abandon her mother in order to marry Queen Marika and assume the title of secondElden Lord. Ranni and her siblings were thus raised to demigod status by their new stepmother.[11]
Although the Two Fingers had chosen her as Marika's successor, Ranni did not wish to be a puppet for theGreater Willand resented her Empyrean fate. In order to escape it, Ranni stole a fragment of theRune of DeathfromMaliketh, the Black Blade, and through fearsome rite, imbued it into the blades ofNumenassassins close to Queen Marika herself. She also gavea fragmentto her brotherRykardas a last resort, so he could kill Maliketh if necessary.[12]Ranni plotted for the assassins to kill another individual while she simultaneously killed herself, slaying her own body while the other person died in spirit, thus freeing herself from being an Empyrean.[13]
In what would become known as theNight of Black Knives, the assassins murderedGodwyn the Golden, killing him in spirit, while Ranni killed herself in body, transferring her spirit into a doll said to be modeled after the image of her mentor, the Snow Witch.[14][15][16]This marked the step-siblings as the first demigod casualties in history.[17]Ranni's fate and her involvement in the plot remained largely unknown by the denizens of the Lands Between.[18]
At some point after the Night of Black Knives, Queen MarikashatteredtheElden Ring. Ranni claimed aGreat Rune, but appears to have discarded it,[19]and largely remained outside ofthe conflictthat followed. As a consequence of her doll body, Ranni required extended periods of hibernation and withdrew from the world, hiding in theCarian Manorwhile her agents worked to bring about her plan of ridding theLands Betweenof the influence of theGreater Will, allowing her to pursue her divine ascension on her own terms.
Long after the Shattering, when theTarnishedreturn to the Lands Between, Ranni hears of aTarnished championhurtling about on aspectral steedgifted to them byMelina. Ranni approaches them at a site of grace, asking if they indeed have the spectral steed. She'll then give the Tarnished theSpirit Calling Bell, noting Torrent's former master had entrusted her with giving it to the next owner.
The Tarnished champion, for their own purposes, makes their way into the Carian Manor and comes face to face with Ranni once again. Ranni accepts the Tarnished into her service and bids them to find a way intoNokron, hoping to claim its treasure;a weaponwith which she could kill the Two Fingers who had chosen her as an Empyrean. The champion manages find their way into Nokron and secures the city's treasure for Ranni, whereupon she departs toNokstella. The champion finds her there and she compels the champion to rid her of the Shadows sent by the Two Fingers to kill her. With the last Shadow defeated, Ranni rewards her champion with the keys to a chest containinga ringintended to be bestowed to her future consort, and achieves her goal of slaying the Two Fingers.
Should the Tarnished champion find the ring and give it to Ranni, she will take the champion as her new consort, and grant them agreatswordas a symbol of their union. She will reveal to them the full extent of her plan: to succeed Queen Marika as god and usher in her "Age of the Stars", removing herself far from theLands Betweento journey out into the cosmos, allowing its inhabitants to have free will over their own choices and live their lives

name: Godwyn the Golden | Elden Ring Wiki
Godwyn the Goldenis a prominent backgroundcharacterinElden Ring. He was ademigodand the son ofQueen Marika the EternalandGodfrey the First Elden Lord, making him a central member of the royal Golden Lineage. Inthe Night of the Black Knives, he was assassinated byBlack Knife Assassinswith the use of daggers imbued with the Rune of Death, stolen fromMaliketh, the Black Blade. As the first of the demigods to fall, only his soul perished in the attack; his living corpse was entombed deep beneath the Erdtree, where it eventually twisted into the Prince of Death and began spreading Deathroot across the realm. His unprecedented death would precipitate the Shattering, a devastating war between the demigods which would be responsible for much of the current state of the Lands Between.
The rune of death was stolen. And the demigods began to fall, starting with Godwyn the Golden.
Godwyn the Golden was a scion of the so-called "Golden Line", of whichGodrick the Graftedwas the final descendant. Early in his mother's divine reign, theErdtreecame under assault by theAncient Dragons, who had ruled the world before Marika's ascent. The forces of the Erdtree managed to triumph against the ancient dragons, with Godwyn prevailing against the dreadedFortissax, earning the mighty dragon's friendship in the process and beginning theancient dragon cultin Leyndell.
Seeking to be free from her fate as a pawn of the Greater Will, Godwyn's half-sisterLunar Princess Rannistole a fragment of the rune of death, imbuing the weapons of Numen assassins with the rune. Ranni wished to shed her Empyrean body but preserve her spirit, which meant that someone else's spirit would need to die.  Nevertheless, when the assassins fell upon theRoyal Capitaland murdered Godwyn, his soul was destroyed and left only his soulless body behind. He was the first demigod in history to die since the ascension ofMarikato the throne of the Lands Between.
Godwyn's death would be the catalyst for the Shattering of the Elden Ring, plunging the kingdom into chaos without the guidance of theGreater Will. Due to Ranni's ritual, Godwyn's flesh was branded with half of theCursemark of Deathand he became the first ofThose Who Live in Death. His body was laid to rest deep in the roots of the Erdtree, but it would eventually corrupt it, leadingDeathrootto sprout across the Lands Between, causing others to also rise in undeath. These undead worshipped Godwyn as the Prince of Death, believing he would eventually return and lead them. An aspect of Godwyn's corpse appeared in the depths ofStormveil Castleand is responsible for the loss ofRogier's legs. Many figures, including his half-brotherMiquellaand his companionFortissax, tried to cure him of his condition and allow him a proper death (seeGolden Epitaph), but to no avail. Fortissax would also become corrupted because of his failure to defeat the Death within Godwyn (seeRemembrance of the Lichdragon).
The deathbed companionFiawould become a leading figure among Those Who Live in Death, eventually making her way to Godwyn's corpse. Having received the other half of the cursemark from Ranni's discarded body with help of the Tarnished, Fia lay with Godwyn to grant him a second life as the Prince of Death. As a result of their union,Fiaconceived arune, which a Tarnished seeking to become Elden Lord might use to mend the Elden Ring, reimbuing the principle of death within the Golden Order.
Throughout the game, players can encounter Godwyn's corpse in multiple locations. His main body rests at the Prince of Death's Throne, located in a shallow pool of purple water at the base of a tainted root in the Deeproot Depths. Additionally, Godwyn's cadaver surrogates can be found at theFog Rift Catacombs,Scorpion River Catacombs, andStormveil Castle.
There is a statue in the Haligtree of an adult figure hugging the twin empyreansMaleniaandMiquella. This is most likely Godwyn as the crown is too dissimilar to Marika's. Based on the available information, Godwyn was likely to have had a close relationship with the twins.
Godwyn's face appears on the back of some crabs.
A sword made to commemorate the death of Godwyn the Golden, first of the demigods to die.
Infused with the humble prayer of a young boy; "O brother, lord brother, please die a true death."
Cursemark carved into the discarded flesh of Ranni the Witch.Also known as the half-wheel wound of the centipede.
This cursemark was carved at the moment of Death of the first demigod,and should have taken the shape of a circle.
However, two demigods perished at the same time,breaking the cursemark into two half-wheels.
Ranni was the first of the demigods whose flesh perished,while the Prince of Death perished in soul alone.
Remembrance of Lichdragon Fortissax, hewn into the Erdtree.
The power of its namesake can be unlocked by the Finger Reader.Alternatively, it can be used to gain a great bounty of runes.
After Godwyn the Golden became the Prince of Death, the ancient dragon fought long and hard against the Death within its companion. Alas, victory was never achieved and its only reward was corruption.
Incantation that channels the power of the ancient dragonFortissax, now corrupted by Death.Strikes surroundings with a storm of Death lightning.Inflicts Death blight upon foes.Charging extends duration of the storm.It is said that this golden lightning was wielded by Godwyn, whobefriended Fortissax.
One of the incantations of the capital's ancient dragon cult. Summons a lightning spear and hurls it before the caster.Charging causes a lightning bolt to strike the point of impact.Long ago, Godwyn the Golden defeated the ancient dragon Fortissax, and befriended his fallen foe — an event that gave rise to the ancient dragon cult in the capital.
On a night of wint'ry fog, the rune of Death was stolen. And the demigods began to fall, starting with Godwyn the Golden.
Godwyn the Goldenwas ademigodand son ofQueen Marika the EternalandGodfrey, First Elden Lord. On theNight of Black Knives, he was murdered by theBlack Knife Assassinswho usedritual daggersimbued with a fragment of theRune of Death.[1]
Godwyn was the son ofQueen Marika the Eternaland her consort and firstElden Lord,Godfrey, making him a scion of the so-called "Golden Lineage", of whichGodrick the Graftedwas the final descendant.[2]
During his mother's reign, theErdtreecame under assault by the Dragons,[3]who had ruled the world before Marika's ascent. The forces of the Erdtree managed to triumph against the dragons, with Godwyn prevailing against the dreadedFortissax, earning the mighty dragon's friendship in the process.[4]
This friendship between former foes led to the establishment ofthe capital’s Ancient Dragon Cult,[5]in which Leyndell Knights could learn dragon incantations. Fortissax’s own sister, the dragonLansseax, took the form of a human to commune with the knights as a priestess of the cult.[6]The cult was allowed within theGolden Ordersince itsseal, and lightning itself, were both imbued with gold.[7]The red-hued incantations were also taught in secret.[8][9]
Godwyn would eventually meet his end during the Night of Black Knives.[10]Seeking to be free from her fate as a pawn of theGreater Will, Godwyn's step-sisterLunar Princess Rannistole a fragment of theRune of DeathfromMaliketh, imbuing the weapons ofNumenassassins with it through a fearsome rite.[11]His death was the first recorded death of a demigod, and served as the catalyst for the shattering of the Elden Ring and the subsequentwarthat broke out between his siblings and stepsiblings.
While Godwyn was believed to be the first dead among the demigods, he and Ranni both died at the same time. As a result, each was branded with one half of theCursemark of Death. Ranni's flesh perished while Godwyn perished in soul alone.[12]He was buried at the Erdtree's roots belowLeyndell,[13]but as he was lacking a soul, his body was unable to die a true death.[14]Some, including his younger half-brotherMiquella[15][16]and his companion Fortissax, tried to cure him of his condition and allow him a proper death, but to no avail. The ancient dragon Fortissax would unsuccessfully try to fight against the Death within Godwyn, but was ultimately corrupted by the blight, becoming a Lichdragon.[17]Godwyn's personal guard became known as theDeath Knights, and quested for their master's cadaver surrogates[18], which would lead them to the catacombs of theRealm of Shadow.
The living body, lacking a soul and unable to die a true death, transformed into an unrecognisable abberation, and became known as the Prince of Death.Deathrootsprouted from it, spreading across the Lands Between through the roots of the Erdtree, and giving rise toThose Who Live in Death.[19]
The deathbed companionFiawould become a leading figure among Those Who Live in Death, eventually making her way to thePrince's throne. With the help from aTarnished champion, Fia gathers the other two halves of the cursemark, one from Ranni's discarded body and the other from Godwyn's body, and she then lays with Godwyn to grant him a second life as the Prince of Death. As a result of their union, Fia conceived arunewhich a champion seeking to become Elden Lord mightuse to mendtheElden Ring, introducing the principle of life within death into theGolden Order.[20]

The game was in production since early 2017 soon after a the DLC, Ringed City, for Dark Souls 3 was released. Both Elden Ring and Sekiro: Shadows Die Twice were being developed simulnateiously by assigned co directors to the games. Since then, the game's release has been delayed a few times, but the first reveal Ttrailer was shown during E3 2019 without an official release date. It was then set to release in around November of 2020, but was agains delayed. After a few more delays it was finally released for all platforms onFebruary 25th of 2022. name: Stats | Elden Ring Wiki
StatisticsinElden Ringrefer to various properties that govern your character's strengths and weaknesses, as well as how they are affected by interactions in and out of combat. There are 8 main Stats in Elden Ring, as well as several dozen secondary stats which all contribute to your character's growth and effectiveness in various situations. Stats are affected by a number of things and can be modified by yourLevel,Equipment, and any active buffs and effects.
Within the Status Menu, you can check your level, attributes, base stats, and more. The information shown here also reflects changes to your attack, defense, and resistances bestowed by armaments and armor that you have equipped.
SeeLevelingfor details on how to level, a breakdown of runes necessary per level, and more.
SeeCalculating Damagefor in depth information regarding dealing damage.
SeeRunesfor details on acquiring runes and rune acquisition boosting equipment.
SeeRebirthfor details on how to reallocate (respec) assigned attribute points.
The primary way to increase your character's stats in Elden Ring is by leveling up. Early in the game, soon after you encounterMelinafor the first time, you'll gain access to the ability to level up by spendingRunes. Runes are earned by defeating enemies and can be used to strengthen your character.
In Elden Ring, there are eight main stats, also known as attributes:Vigor,Mind,Endurance,Strength,Dexterity,Intelligence,Faith, andArcane. Each of these attributes has a significant impact on your character’s secondary stats, such as HP (health points), FP (focus points), Stamina, and Equipment Load. By spending Runes at aSite of Grace, you can increase these primary stats, which not only raises your character's overall level but also boosts your secondary stats — making your character more powerful and better suited to face the challenges ahead.
Additionally, your stats can be influenced by the equipment you have equipped and any active buffs from magic or items. Successfully combining and optimizing these elements is crucial for character development and creating effective builds that will help you progress through the game. Understanding how these various factors interact allows players to craft a character that matches their playstyle and is capable of overcoming the diverse challenges in Elden Ring.
After completingRaya Lucaria Academy, you will gain the ability to reset your point allocations and redistribute all of your earned stat points however you wish. This process requires aLarval Tear, a rare item obtainable through various means. To re-specialize (respec), simply interact withRennalaand exchange a Larval Tear. By the time you reach this point, you'll likely be over level 50, making your early build choices important since they can't be changed until now. For ideas on creating a powerful character, check out our Elden RingBuildspage.
This mechanic, known as "Respeccing," lets players customize and experiment with different builds without having to restart the game.
A cumulative figure that represents overall attribute strength.You can level up using runes.
Total runes in possession. Upon dying, you will drop any runes in your possession at the site of your death.
Number of runes required to raise a level.When you Level Up, you can choose an attribute to increase.
This section lists all of your character's Main Stats, also referred to asAttributes. These Stats govern all other secondary Stats and can be increased by spending acquiredRuneson them using the Level Up menu at anySite of Grace, once the feature is unlocked.
At certain points when leveling an Attribute to higher values, you will start getting diminishing returns. i.e. the benefit you gain from leveling that Stat is less significant than before. The values at which these diminishing returns begin are referred to as soft-caps or breakpoints. You can find the soft-cap of each Attribute listed below. Note that some stats actually grant accelerating returns at lower levels: for example, Vigor's HP gain per level increases from levels 1-40, but decreases after level 40.
The hard-cap for all Stats is 99: you are unable to level a Stat past that level, and it is not possible to exceed 99 through equipment or buffs. (An exception is that your effective Strength can be increased past 99 by two-handing.)
Attribute governingHP.Also affects fire resistance andImmunitystat.
Scaling accelerates until 40.Soft-capped at 40 / 60.
Attribute governingFP.Also affects theFocusstat.
WeaponsandArmorStats provide useful information about the benefits provided by the equipment.

The degree to which incomingSlashing Physical Damageis negated.
The degree to which incomingPiercing Physical Damageis negated.
The degree to which incomingMagic Damageis negated.
The degree to which incomingFire Damageis negated.
The degree to which incomingLightning Damageis negated.
The degree to which incomingHoly Damageis negated.
About Deathis anInfo IteminELDEN RING(2022).
Upon dying, you will be revived at the last site of grace that you visited.
You will drop any runes in your possession at the site of your death.
If you die again before reclaiming those runes, they will be lost forever.
The compass at the top of the screen indicates the direction of the lost runes.

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Grace
This tiny golden aura is the grace of the Erdtree. [...] The rays of grace, that guide you through your burden.
Grace(祝福,Shukufuku), also referred to as theGrace of Gold(黄金の祝福,Ōgon no Shukufuku),[1][2][3]is a blessing given to people throughout theLands Betweenby theElden Ringand theErdtreethat symbolizes its presence.[4]This blessing is represented by a golden light in the eyes of the inhabitants of the Lands Between.[5]Those who had grace bestowed on them, but later lost it, are known asTarnished.[6]
The Lands Between are blessed by the presence of the Elden Ring and by the Erdtree, which symbolizes its presence, and this has given grace or blessing to the people throughout the land, great and small.[5]
At some point,Queen Marika the Eternaltook away Grace fromGodfrey, First Elden Lordand his kinfolk, turning them into Tarnished. They then left the  Lands Between in an event called the Long March of the Tarnished.[7]Long afterwards, Grace would be returned to them, or their descendants, and they would be called back to the Lands Between.
At the time of the game, when given back, Grace itself is what gives the Tarnished their life.[8]
Sometimes, the Tarnished can see golden rays of Grace that point in a particular direction, called the Guidance of Grace. It exists to guide the Tarnished and lead them along the proper path. It was also said that the guidance of grace would ensure that aFinger Maidenbe brought to her chosen Tarnished. Or at least, such was the promise long ago.[9]
Even now, some sites of grace retain that power, and their golden rays can guide the Tarnished along the way.[10]
It is said that true guidance awaits those with iron wills and unwavering faith,[11]although it can be lost.[12][13][14]In fact, most Tarnished don't even see it nowadays.[15]
Those in distant lands who saw the guidance of grace were usually seen as undesirables, and were usually expatriated, after which they set to journey to the Lands Between.[16][17]Similarly, the churches outside the Lands Between, dedicated to the teachings of the Two Fingers, sentconfessorsout to follow the guidance of grace.

name: The Gloam-Eyed Queen
The Gloam-Eyed Queen cradles newborn apostles swaddled in this cloth. Soon they will grow to become the death of the gods.
The Gloam-Eyed Queenwas anEmpyreanwho was defeated long ago byMaliketh. She was the leader of theGodskin Apostlesand wielded the god-slaying power ofDestined Death.[1][2][3]
The Gloam-Eyed Queen was an Empyrean chosen by her ownTwo Fingers. She led the apostles in their god hunt,[3]wielded the power ofDestined Deathand channeling itsBlack Flamesthrough herGodslayer's Greatsword.[1]She cradled newborn Godskin Apostles in aswaddling clothmade from patches of supple skin sewn together.[4]Her apostles developed inhuman physiology and would grow to be the death of the gods.[5]
Queen Marikadesired the removal of theRune of Deathfrom theElden Ringto create theGolden Order.[6]After the Gloam-Eyed Queen and her apostles were defeated at the hands ofMaliketh, the Rune of Death was sealed away within hisBlack Bladeand the true power of theGodslayer incantationswas lost.[7][8][9]The Gloam-Eyed Queen's sword was locked away at the bottom of theDivine Tower of Caelid, and her fate remains unknown.

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Fell God
The fell god still lurks within the Fire Giants.
Thefell god,[1]also known as theone-eyed god,[2]is anunseen characterinELDEN RING(2022). It is the source of theGiants' FlameandGiants' Flame Incantations.
The fell god is an ancientdeityworshiped by theFire Giants. It is commonly referred to with a myriad of derogatory terms by the inhabitants of theLands Between, such as the "corrupt", "grotesque", "malformed", "fell" or "evil" god of the Fire Giants. It is represented in the visage of a single eye with a fiery-orange iris and nine pupils within.
It physically manifests itself in the shape of a grotesque face in the torsos of its followers, channeling its power through them, its greatest flames emerging from its mouth (commonly located in the host giant's stomach) along with the undying flames found seeded within theirgiant black forgeenabling its followers to develop innumerable fireincantations.
The fell god of fire has been around for a long time and predates theErdtree. It was a dreaded figure in the old legends of thehornsentofEnir-Ilim.[3]It was worshiped by the Fire Giants,[2]who it cursed for eternity to tend the Flame within theForge of the Giants.[1]
The powers of the Flame were once deemed as a threat to the Erdtree byQueen Marikaand theGolden Orderand thus they waged a bloodyWar Against the Giants. Once the Fire Giants were defeated,[1]Queen Marika realized the fires of their forge could not die and thus sealed it away,[4]reducing its once formidable flame into mere embers and cursing the last surviving Fire Giant to keep them so for all eternity.[5]
Even then, after countless years, innumerableProphetswould be haunted by visions of its flames consuming the Erdtree.[6]And the one-eyed god still lurks dormant within its subjects,[7]on the cusp of being awakened at any moment with a sufficient sacrificial offering.

TheTwinbirdis a mentioned entity inELDEN RING(2022). It is said to be the envoy of anOuter God, and the mother of theDeathbirds.
The Twinbird is scarcely mentioned in theLands Between. It is portrayed as a two-headed bird with half-red and half-blue or black plumage.
The Twinbird is said to be the envoy of an Outer God, and the mother of the Deathbirds.[1]Its whereabouts are unknown, and only its offspring being seen throughout the Lands Between. The colour of its plumage may be alluded to by the red and blue feathers on theRed-Feathered BranchswordandBlue-Feathered Branchswordused in ancient Death rituals before the age of the Erdtree.[2][3][4]

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Serosh
Serosh, the Beast Regentis acharacterinELDEN RING(2022). He serves asKing Godfrey'sregent and the counselor of his descendants, and can be encountered alongside his Lord at the foot of the burningErdtreeinLeyndell, Ashen Capital.
Serosh was a large, goldenlionknown as the Lord ofBeasts.[1]Among thebeastmenofFarum Azula, the presence of five fingers was celebrated as a symbol of theintelligencegranted to their kind, and the five black nails on theBeastclaw Greathammerare believed to represent Serosh.[1][2]
Serosh was taken uponGodfrey's back when he vowed to become a lord, suppressing his ceaseless lust for battle, and became known as his Beast Regent.[1][3]Serosh went on to serve as a counselor guiding Godfrey's offspring, theGolden Lineageand became a longstanding symbol of the Golden Lineage, representing a bygone era of glory.[4][5]General Radahn, captivated by Godfrey in his youth, worearmordepicting a golden lion, said to symbolize both Godfrey and Serosh.[6]
Serosh remained with Godfrey even after he becameTarnishedand was exiled from theLands Between,[7]and appears to have perished alongside Godfrey in theBadlands.
Following theShattering, when theGuidance of Gracewas restored to the Tarnished, Serosh returned to the Lands Between alongside Godfrey. At the foot of the burningErdtree, the former Elden Lord was confronted by aTarnished. During the battle, Serosh began to take on a more tangible form, seemingly preparing to play active role in the fight. However, Godfrey stopped Serosh, thanked him for his service, before killing him. Covered in the blood of his former regent, Godfrey discarded hisaxeand continued to fight as Hoarah Loux before being defeated.
As a lion, the hair on Serosh's face, upper arms and torso are a dark gray color, while the long fur on his mane and forearms are a silvery white. He has silver-colored plate-mail on his chest and shoulders, with matching sharp-tipped gauntlets covering his five-fingered hands.
The skin on his snout and lips are both colored black and his face is covered in scars, the most notable ones crossing over his perpetually closed eyes; potentially indicating blindness. The largest having cleaved through the left side of his silver crown, before continuing down-right of his forehead and over his right eye before ending at the bottom his right cheek.
While mounted on Godfrey's back, Serosh's body appears translucent, and the lower half of his body is not visible.

The Numen are said to have come from outside the Lands Between, and are in fact of the same stock as Queen Marika herself.
The Numen are the descendants of denizens from another world. They are long lived but seldom born.[1]
The Numen are said to have come from outside the Lands Between from a place known only as 'the lands of the Numen',[2]and are in fact the same stock asQueen Marikaherself.[3]The hammer with which Marika shattered theElden Ring, andRadagonattempted to repair it, was made in the lands of the Numen.[2]
TheBlack Knife Assassinswho murderedGodwyn the Goldenduring theNight of Black Kniveswere all women rumored to be Numen who had close ties to Queen Marika,[4]as well as scions ofthe Eternal City.[5]

name: Nox
The Nox are the inhabitants of the Eternal Cities ofNokronandNokstella. They are a grey-skinned, cold-blooded race known for wielding flowing weapons[1]forged from the liquid metal ofSilver Tears.
Long ago, the Nox committed treason against theGreater Willand its vassalFingers, fashioning crystalline helmets out of glass to ward off their intervention.[2]However, they invoked the ire of the Greater Will and were banished deep underground, forced to live under a false night sky in eternal anticipation of the coming age of stars, and of their Lord of Night.[3]
Monks clad in armour with silk capes and hoods. They wield Flowing Hammers which can elongate in a whip-like fashion for additional range, turn into semi-spherical spiked fist weapons which they dual-wield, or into single, spherical weapons resembling censers.
Can include a separate table for a specific instance of this variant's moveset.
Skilled swordstresses of the Eternal Cities, who serve as the personal guards of the Nightmaidens, and wear conical crowns with silk veils that cover their eyes.[4]They wield flowing curved swords which can elongate for additional range. They are sometimes seen ridingGiant Ants.
Nox who hold the highest clerical rank, symbolised by their twin crowns, which hide their eyes with silk.[5]They use short, curved daggers in combat, and can create a life-sappingmist.
A duo consisting of a Monk and a Swordstress. They are found in a courtyard on the northern side of Sellia, behind a magical seal which can be broken by lighting three braziers atop towers throughout the town. Inside the courtyard is a large chair, reminiscent of those found in the Eternal Cities, albeit without a giant skeleton occupying it. A chest beneath the chair, accessible only once the duo has been defeated, containsLusat's Glintstone Staff.

name: Albinauric | Elden Ring Wiki
AlbinauricsareHumanoid EnemiesinElden Ring.Albinauricsare said to have been artificial lifeforms that were made by humans.
First-Generation Albinauricshave a human-like appearance and a flawed pair of legs, which eventually give out and sometimes even disappear.
Second-Generation Albinauricsare short creatures, with smooth gray skin and dumpy heads resembling those of frogs. They use primitive weapons such as wooden clubs and makeshift shields, and they often congregate in large groups. Second-GenerationAlbinauricsare very agile and able to cartwheel around.
A First-GenerationAlbinauriccan be summoned using the Spirit AshLatenna The Albinauric. A pair of Second-GenerationAlbinauricscan be summoned using theAlbinauric Ashes.
Albinaurics are lifeforms made by human hands. Thus, many believe them to live impure lives, untouched by the Erdtree's grace.
Several First-GenerationAlbinauricVillagers can still be found moaning inside theVillage of the Albinauricsin southwest Liurnia. Some First-GenerationAlbinauricMages can be found past the bridge leading away from the Village's well. [Map Link]
The player must encounterAlbus, an NPC and First-GenerationAlbinauricVillager, in order to reach theConsecrated Snowfield. He is found in the Village of the Albinaurics, disguised as a large pot. It is recommended that the player defeat the nearbyDepraved Perfumerbefore speaking to him.
Just outside of the Village of the Albinaurics, two Afflicted First-GenerationAlbinauricscoughing up clouds ofPoisoncan be found kneeling on the bank of the Poison swamp below the Village.
Plenty of First-GenerationAlbinauricMages can be found on the ground level ofCaria Manor.
Several First-GenerationAlbinauricscan be found in the dungeon ofVolcano Manor.
A few Insane First-GenerationAlbinauricscan be found in the lower levels ofLeyndell Royal Capital, near the well that leads down into theSubterranean Shunning-Grounds.
A few First-GenerationAlbinauricscan be found inCastle Sol, in the room leading up to the area immediately preceding the Boss Arena.
One First-GenerationAlbinauric Archercan be found near the entrance to the Consecrated Snowfield, just outside the end of theHidden Path to the Haligtree, riding herDirewolf.
Several First-GenerationAlbinauricArchers can be found outside to the south ofOrdina, Liturgical Townin the Consecrated Snowfield. One rides a Direwolf.
Second-GenerationAlbinauricscan be found all overLiurnia of the Lakes. Groups of them often roam the ruins of theAcademy Gate Town. [Map Link]
Several Second-GenerationAlbinauricscan be found outside to the east ofOrdina, Liturgical Townin theConsecrated Snowfield, and more leading up to theMinor Erdtree.
A large amount of red Second-GenerationAlbinauricswith 3 small Omen horns on their forehead can be found in theMohgwyn Palacearea, with many variations of weapons and equipment. In the forested area, the red Second-GenerationAlbinauricsthat blow theirCurved Great Clublike a horn can summon aGiant Skeleton (Spirit), which is the upper half of a colossal skeleton usually summoned byTibia Mariners.
There are two types:First-Generation AlbinauricsandSecond-Generation Albinaurics.
Upon reachingMohgwyn Palace, one can fast travel to the Palace Approach Ledge-Road site of grace, equip theSacred Relic Swordto use theWave of Goldweapon skill and farmAlbinaurics. Effectively yielding up to6,000,000Runesper hour with theGolden ScarabTalisman.
Though some Albinaurics wield aRipple BladeorShamshir, they do not drop them.
My legs will soon fade, and with them, my life. Alas, this is the immovable fate of all Albinaurics.
TheAlbinauricsare a man-made species encountered inELDEN RING(2022).
The albinaurics are artificial life found across theLands Betweeneither as aFirst-Generation Albinauric(including anarcher variant) orSecond-Generation Albinauric.
Albinaurics are lifeforms made by human hands. Thus, many believe them to live impure lives, untouched by the Erdtree's grace.[1]They are said to have been created from a primordial drop of dew[2], and secretly harbour the ability to cast magic using their innate arcaneness.[3]All Albinaurics share a fate; their legs will one day fade, and with them, their lives.[4]This process can be seen most clearly in the elderly, bearded Albinaurics that inhabit theVillage of the Albinaurics.
Albinaurics are viewed as impure, and are persecuted by theKnights of the Cuckoofor their defiled blood.[5]They seek salvation inMiquella's Haligtree, which they believe to be their chosen land.[6]Aged Albinaurics carryIvory Sicklesin dedication to the Haligtree, despite having never entered its presence.[7]
All first-generation Albinaurics are disabled and have lost the use of their legs. The males appear as withered old men with long beards whose legs are vanishing into shadow. The female archers, who wear blue silver mail born from the same mother as themselves[8], also lack the functionality of their legs, which they compensate for by riding wolfback. Nonetheless, they were feared as deadly sharpshooters.[9]
Second-generation Albinaurics differ visually from the more humanoid first generation specimens, having heads that resemble those of frogs[10]and protruding bellies.[11]They wield weaponry modelled after the ripples that are said to be the origin of their species[12][13], as well as wooden clubs shaped like the crescent moon.[14][15]
Albinaurics are encountered throughout theLands Between. A majority may be found in centralLiurnia.
Albinaurics are also found in theRealm of Shadow.

name: Omen | Elden Ring Wiki
Omenis a type ofMonster EnemyinElden Ring.Omenare curse-born, ogre-like beings that favor using large and heavy weapons such asGreatswordsorGreataxes. They are normally slow moving and can often be found sleeping or otherwise distracted.Omenwill, however, move surprisingly fast and erupt with great ferocity when provoked, jumping into battle with multiple wide swings and attacks.Omenborn to commoners often have their horns excised (cut off), generally ending in the child's death, whileOmenborn toNobilityare allowed to retain their gnarled horns, but are hidden away underground to live in obscurity.
Stormveil CastleYou can find the Omen at the heavily guarded courtyard of the castle. The nearest checkpoint is theLiftside Chamber Site of Grace.
You can find the Omen at the heavily guarded courtyard of the castle. The nearest checkpoint is theLiftside Chamber Site of Grace.
There is one near the end ofUnsightly Catacombs.
Minor Erdtree (Capital Outskirts) guardingTwiggy Cracked TearandCrimson Crystal Tear. This Omen can useFia's Mist, just like theCommonersaccompanying it. The Commoners also all wear a small face shroud, suggesting a relationship to Deathbed Companions, or perhapsFiaherself.
Capital Outskirts: TwoOmensappear as the field bossFell Twins.
The absorption numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example if an absorption is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% is absorbed. Bigger number = less damage. An absorption of 100 means no damage goes through, and a resistance of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of whatever aux buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs.
One of the few enemies that are attracted toShadow Bait.
Sleeping Omen can sometimes be found inAltus Plateau. They appear to be suffering from nightmares, convulsing and writhing around in their sleep.
There are two variants, those with cut horns, and those with uncut horns, and each variant can carry either anOmen Cleaveror aWarped Axe. The uncut horn variant can summon wraiths and have some moves that have black-and-gold cursed flames, like theRevenantsandWraith Callers.
Omenkillersmay have been created to cull the Omen population. TheOmensmirk Maskare said to be in imitation of the evil spirits in the Omen’s nightmares.
Uses FP to unleash wraiths that chase down foes.
Omen babies have all their horns excised, causing most to perish.These fetishes are made to memorialize them.
"Please, don't hate me, or curse me. Please."
Doll of a curseborn bairn from the Erdtree's royal line.
Uses FP to unleash many wraiths that chase down foes.
Omen babies born of royalty do not have their horns excised, but instead are kept underground, unbeknownst to anyone, imprisoned for eternity.
These memorial fetishes are fashioned in secret.
Heavy-bladed curved sword of colossal size awarded to Omen as a tool of war. This weapon is made to take advantage of brute strength.
TheOmen(忌み,Imi,or 忌み子,Imigo) are accursed beings found in theLands Betweenborn without the grace of theErdtree.[1]
The Omen are hulking and brutish in appearance, covered in twisted horns growing from their body. Certain Omen, such asMorgott, the Omen KingandMohg, Lord of Bloodalso have tails and feathered wings. These traits are reminiscent of the vestiges of the Crucible, considered a signifier of the divine in ancient times, but reviled as an impurity as civilization advanced.[2]
Omen babies have all their horns excised, which causes most to perish; they are memorialized with small fetish dolls in the likeness of an infant Omen with their horns cut off.[3]Meanwhile, Omen born to royalty keep their horns, but are kept underground, unbeknownst to anyone, where they are bound by shackles for eternity.[4]Fetish dolls depicting the Omen infant with their horns left intact are crafted in secret to memorialize these Omen.[5]Wraithserupt from the bodies of Omen whose horns remain intact, and can also be expelled via the breath, or used to enwreathe their weapons.
Omen are seen as impure due to their cursed blood.[6][7]For this reason they are hunted byOmenkillers,  the first of which was the perfumerRollo, who wield giant cleavers comprised of amputated Omen horns that cause blood loss,[8]and wear masks imitating the evil spirits that haunt the Omen in their nightmares.[9]The perfumerTriciaand her associates[6]dedicated their efforts to treating Omen, among others seen as impure. When her efforts failed, she instead became their companion when they died, ensuring they could pass peacefully.[10]
Despite being reviled, excised Omen are sometimes used as soldiers. They are awarded cleavers of colossal size, taking advantage of the Omen's brute strength. However, the blades are etched with a remnant of a deteriorative malediction to ensure that the blade can be taken away.[11]They occasionally can be found wearing black cloaks, and certain Omen among these cloaked variants have taken to worshiping thePrince of Death.

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Dragon Communion | Elden Ring Wiki
Dragon Communionis a seldom-known practice inElden Ring. It involves feasting on the remains ofDragonsin order to gain their powers and features.Dragon Heartsare required in order to be exchanged forDragon Communion Incantationsat select locations in the game. After obtaining 4 spells in this manner, the tarnished's eyes will turn draconic, which can be undone at Fia's Mirror inRoundtable Hold. Theenemiesthat drop Dragon Hearts include named dragons,Glintstone Dragons,Magma Wyrms(includingMakarandTheodorix),Ghostflame DragonsandJagged Peak Drakes.
Those who partake in Dragon Communion will one day shed their humanity." - Yura
Dragon Communion began as a practice developed as a retaliatory effort byDragonlord PlacidusaxagainstBayle the Dreadand his brood in an age long past. Bayle had attacked Placidusax and after the two sustained serious injuries, Bayle fled to theJagged Peak. Followers of Placidusax would encourage warriors to slay dragons and consume their flesh, marking the beginning of the drake warriors and knights. One such follower wasFlorissax, who gave up her dragon form to guide prospective drake warriors as theDragon Communion Priestess. Due to her choice in attire, it can be assumed thatEleonora, Violet Bloody Fingerwas one of drake knights who took part in Dragon Communion as she also wields the incantations in battle.Banished Knightsalso have a connection to this practice and serving theAncient Dragonsas some use Dragon Commuion spells and theirhelmshave a dragon motif. TheShadow of the Erdtree DLCalso introducesIgon, a drake warrior who has been grievously injured in a confrontation with Bayle and will aid the tarnished in Bayle's defeat.
Aweaknessdragons possess, and exploited by drake warriors, is to weapons and equipment made withgravel stone, the material that comprises the scales of their ancient ancestors. After letting their hunger from Dragon Communion go unchecked, drake warriors' bodies would gradually change shape. With theRock Heartitem, one can transform their appearance to become more dragon-like while increasing the power of Dragon Communion incantations. TheAncient Dragon-Manmakes use of this item, and he was once an accomplished drake warrior before turning to Bayle's side in theDragon's Pit. The end result of the hubris of Dragon Communion areMagma Wyrms, which are said to be once human heroes who partook in Dragon Communion, only to become terrifying monsters who were cursed to crawl the earth upon their bellies, shadows of their former selves.Great Wyrm Theodorixwas formerly aTrollwarrior and hero of the War against the Giants who took part in Dragon Communion, proving that humans were not the only practitioners.
On a small tucked-away island far off the western coast ofLimgrave, this church can only be accessed by going through theCoastal Caveand defeating theDemi-Human Chiefs.Bloody Finger Hunter Yurawill direct the player here if they manage to defeatFlying Dragon Agheelbefore he leaves the lake area.
In southwesternCaelidlies a broken-down cathedral devoted to Dragon Communion, and it is still closely guarded by some surroundingBanished Knights. Not too far up the road from it isEkzykes, Dragon Communion Revenger, who is hostile to all who come near.
Near theFoot of the Jagged Peakand past theDragon's Pitlies the corpse of an enormous dead dragon and from it a large altar has been made for Dragon Communion. Players will meet theDragon Communion Priestesshere who will encourage them to pursue and slayBayle the Dread, so that they might feast upon hisheartand unlock a powerful incantation of their choice.

Dragon Communion(竜餐,Ryūsan) is a ritual inELDEN RING(2022). It involves the hunting ofdrakes, the descendants ofAncient Dragons, and the consumption of theirgravel stone-coveredhearts.
Specifically,Dragon Communionis the act of consuming dragon hearts in order to acquire thedraconic powerswithin. The hearts are consumed at aDragon Communion Altarin the presence of a fallen dragon.
In the distant past, the lord of theancient dragons,Placidusax, was attacked by the great drake,Bayle the Dread. Their clash ended in a stalemate and left both gravely wounded, with Bayle fleeing the field of battle.[1]
As punishment for Bayle's transgression, the Ancient Dragons established the practice of Dragon Communion. One of Placidusax's followers, Florissax, took mortal form asa humanoid priestessto spread the ritual.[2]Warriors were lured to this cause with the promise of great power which could only be acquired by consuming the heart of a drake.[3][4]
As time passed, the practice would continue without influence from the priestesses; many practitioners would forget the original purpose of the hunt and would simply carry on consuming hearts in pursuit of greater power.[citation needed]Some drakes have become aware of this practice, such asEkzykes the Decaying, who even after succumbing toMalenia'srotwould never forget his hatred and thus keeps himself stationed at the entrance of theCathedral of Dragon Communion, so that he may kill or deter any would-be practitioners before they can reach the altar[5].
Dragon Communion practitioners develop a hunger for the hearts as they hunt, which gradually intensifies as they devour more hearts. This leads some to commune without restraint, causing their bodies and minds to become increasingly wyrm-like.[6]The end-result is the full transformation intoMagma Wyrms, dragon-like creatures with pitifully small wings, incapable of flight and cursed to crawl the earth on their bellies until the end of their days.[7]Ironically, this end often comes at the hands of their fellow practitioners as their own hearts become fair game for communion.

name: Ancient Dragons | Elden Ring Wiki
Ancient Dragonsare a type of flyingenemyinElden Ring. Long before theErdtreeandQueen Marika, they were part of the ruling force of the Lands Between fromCrumbling Farum Azulaand have bodies ofGravel Stoneand armies ofBeastmenwho worship them. Most of them serve as formidableBossesfor the tarnished to defeat and wield deadly lightning as their weapons. For unnamedAncient Dragons, seeFarum Azula Dragons.Dragonsare considered their lesser descendants.
Spoken of in legend, red lightning is the weapon wielded by the ancient dragons.
Dragonlord Placidusax ruled Farum Azula before the age of the Erdtree. According to hisRemembrance, he was once an Elden Lord in a forgotten time, but once his god fled he continues to wait for their return in a storm beyond time. Even hisscalesseem to have time-altering properties that can allow weapons to become capable of slaying a god. Numerous Ancient Dragons would protect their lord during his slumber by becoming a wall of living rock. Unlike the rest of his kin, he at one point possessed four heads. Placidusax would lose two heads and receive other grievous injuries after an attack fromBayle the Dread, but not without inflicting more damage onto his mortal foe. In retaliation to Bayle's betrayal, Dragonlord Placidusax had his followers encourage warriors to partake inDragon Communion, and to hunt down Bayle's brood in order to feast on their hearts. Note that for the purposes of beingweakto certain weapons and items, Placidusax does not count as an Ancient Dragon.
Ancient Dragon Gransax was a creature of immense size who assailedLeyndell, Royal Capitalwhich started a conflict between the Ancient Dragons and its inhabitants. Gransax wielded aspearinfused with lightning into battle and upon its death its body became immovable stone that was left in Leyndell as a permanent fixture of the city. This attack would inspire someTree Sentinelsto take ondraconicfeatures, according to theMalformed Dragon Set.
Ancient Dragon Lansseax is the sibling of Fortissax and took part in the war between the Ancient Dragons and Leyndell. Lansseax wielded aglaiveof red lightning and after the war's conclusion took the form of a human to teach knightsincantationsas a member of theAncient Dragon Cultin the royal capital. Out of all the knights, she lovedVykethe most, who was a contender to become Elden Lord. She can still be found roaming aroundStormcaller ChurchinAltus Plateau.
Ancient Dragon Fortissax, also known as the Lichdragon and the mightiest boulderstone, is the sibling of Lansseax and took part in the war between the Ancient Dragons and Leyndell. Fortissax wielded dualspearsof red lightning and was defeated byGodwyn the Goldenon the final battlefield of the conflict. Godwyn then befriended Fortissax, giving rise to the Ancient Dragon cult in Leyndell. According to theRemembrance of the Lichdragon, Fortissax fought against the affliction that had taken over its deceased comrade, but ultimately failed to save him and became corrupted.
Ancient Dragon Florissax, also known as the Dragon Communion Priestess, is a potential ally encountered in theShadow of the ErdtreeDLC. Each night she offers her sleep to her lord Placidusax, and is susceptible to a sleep inducingtonic. Florissax has been enticing young warriors to partake in Dragon Communion from theGrand Altar of Dragon Communionnear theFoot of the Jagged Peak. She encourages the tarnished to seek outBayle the Dreadto kill him and consumehis hearton behalf of her lord.
Ancient Dragon Senessax is a powerful foe encountered in theShadow of the ErdtreeDLC. Found before reaching the summit ofJagged Peak, it is likely Senessax was one of the Ancient Dragons who sided with the betrayer over their lord Placidusax as mentioned in thered lightning potdescription. Senessax is especially dangerous given the close-by small bodies of water that can increaselightning damageagainst the tarnished.

Ancient Dragonis an enemy inELDEN RING(2022).
The Ancient Dragons ruled in the prehistoric era before theErdtree.[1]They wielded red lightning as a weapon[2], and had scales made of sharp, pointed gravel stones.[3]They were ruled over byDragonlord Placidusax, said to have beenElden Lordin the time before the Erdtree[4], from the royal city ofFarum Azula[5], and it is said that they would protect their lord as a wall of living rock.[6]
Ancient Dragons have light grey bodies resembling stone. They possess four legs, as well as four wings inlayed with gold, distinguishing them from theirlesser descendants. They have short, flat muzzles, orange-yellow eyes, and wispy grey hairs along their backs. They can breathe fire like many of their descendants, however they also possess the ability to wield red lightning, which often manifests in the form of spears and glaives.
During the reign ofQueen Marika the Eternal, the Ancient Dragon Gransax wrought havoc onLeyndell, Royal Capital, the only time in recorded history that Leyndell's walls have fallen.[7]This marked the dawn of the war against the Dragons, during which the Tree Sentinels clad themselves in armor resembling the bodies of the Dragons in order to protect the Erdtree.[8]During this conflictGodwyn the Goldenfought to the last against the Ancient DragonFortissax.[9]Godwyn defeated Fortissax, however he befriended his fallen foe, ending the conflict and giving rise to the capital's Ancient Dragon Cult.[10]Worship of the Ancient Dragons does not conflict with faith in the Erdtree, as the Dragons' lightning is imbued with gold, and as such the Cult was permitted within Leyndell.[11]
Ancient Dragons are greatly resistant toStancedamage. In addition to their base 120 Stance health, they only take 20% Stance damage (effectively giving them 600 Stance health against those hits) from hits against everything except for their heads, though their heads at least take doubled Stance damage compared to the rest of their body (effectively giving them 300 Stance health against those hits). Though their Stance health won't refill unless they haven't taken Stance damage for a fairly lengthy 9.231 seconds, this, in addition to how hard their heads can be to hit, make them sturdy foes.
Can include a separate table for a specific instance of this variant's moveset.
Lansseax, the sister of Fortissax, is said to have taken the form of a human priestess in order to commune with the knights of the Ancient Dragon Cult.[12]Her most beloved knight wasVykethe dragonspear[13], a Tarnished knight of theRoundtable Hold, who was later scourged by the frenzied flame.[14]
Lansseax is first encountered near the Abandoned Coffin Site of Grace, near the entrance to Altus Plateau from theRuin-Strewn Precipice. After sustaining enough damage, she will fly away. She can later be encountered on a hill just south-west of the Rampartside Path Site of Grace in the east of Altus Plateau, where she can be defeated for good.

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Fire Giant
O trifling giant, mayest thou tend thy flame for eternity.
TheFire Giantis abossinELDEN RING(2022). He is encountered atFlame Peakon theMountaintops of the Giants. This encounter isnotoptional as it must be completed to unlockCrumbling Farum Azulaand advance the main storyline.
In the days before theErdtree, the Giants carved out a civilization in the inhospitable mountains to the north, after chasing away theIce Dragonswho had previously ruled it.[1]Here, they worshipped aFell Godand were bound to tend theFlameof their god for eternity.[2]
BeforeQueen Marika the Eternalushered in herAge of the Erdtree, she had her then husband,Godfrey, the firstElden Lord, launch anattackagainst the Giants,[3]fearing that theirfiremight burn herErdtree.[4]
The mighty Giants borrowed the power of their fell god, but were still defeated[2]by Godfrey[5]and hisCrucible Knights,[6]with Marika allegedly striking down the fell god.[7]Only a single Fire Giant remained, and Marika cursed him to forever tend his Flame, ensuring it could not harm her Erdtree.[8]During this time, the Fire Giant crafted a leg brace for a wound on his left leg.
After untold ages of tending the flame, the Fire Giant's vigil is interrupted by aTarnished, seeking to harness the Flame to burn the Erdtree. The Fire Giant fights to crush the champion, but the Tarnished repeatedly strikes at the Giant's legs, slicing apart his leg brace and causing the Giant's left leg to break. In immense pain, the Fire Giant tears off the foot of his broken leg, using it as a sacrifice to unleash the power of the fell god. Despite being on more even terms, the Fire Giant is eventually felled by the Tarnished.
Alexander, Warrior Jaris available as a summon for this fight, provided he has been met atMt. Gelmir. His summon sign is just inside the boss gate.
The arena is a large snowfield with craggy, uneven terrain. The field slops upwards from the entrance, and the Giant begins the fight at the top of the slope. Torrent can be called during this fight, and is useful for covering distance and avoiding the avalanche by jumping.
During phase 1, the Fire Giant will fight using a large, circular dish. Although he is fairly slow-moving, he is able to cover distance using his roll. He also possesses the ability to launch an avalanche straight towards the player. Initially, the majority of his attacks involve slamming the dish into the ground.
The objective initially is to attack the red braids wrapped around his left leg. After enough damage has been dealt, the braids will fall off, uncovering his injured ankle. At this point he will roll three times in succession, and then reach into the mouth on his abdomen, coating his hand in flames. He now gains the ability to use two fire-based abilities- a fast-moving fireball, and a large, slow-moving fire orb that homes in on the player.
Once his health drops below 47%, a cutscene plays and phase 2 begins. The Fire Giant has now lost the large dish as well as his left leg, and is forced to kneel on the ground. He is less mobile during this phase, however he can still roll. He now has a greater variety of fire spells. He may summon pillars of fire that erupt from the ground around him, breathe fire, or spew molten rocks that rain down on the arena. His weak spot is now on his left forearm.

name: Godskin Apostle
Godskin Apostleis a reoccurring boss inELDEN RING(2022).
Lanky humanoids clad in robes sewn together from patches of smooth skin.[1]The Godskin Apostles were led by theGloam-Eyed Queen[2], who cradled them as newborns in a swaddling cloth made from skin much like their robes[3]. They servedDestined Death[1], and wielded god-slaying black flame. However, whenMaliketh, the Black Blade, sealed away the Rune of Death, the flame's true power was lost.[4]
Can include a separate table for a specific instance of this variant's moveset.
See also:Godskin NobleA duo consisting of a Godskin Apostle and Godskin Noble, encountered in the Dragon Temple within Crumbling Farum Azula. They share a health bar, as well as having their own individual health. If one is killed, the other will resurrect them after a short amount of time. If both are killed before the shared health bar reaches 0, the Noble will respawn and summon the Apostle after a short amount of time.

name: Frenzied Flame Proscription | Elden Ring Wiki
Frenzied Flame Proscriptionis aLocationinElden Ring. Theareais found beneathSubterranean Shunning-Grounds, underneath theCathedral of the ForsakenSite of Grace.
Reached upon defeatingMohg, the Omen, atSubterranean Shunning-Grounds.Elden Ring Interactive Map Link. The area is sealed untilMorgott the Omen Kinghas been defeated.
x1Rune Arc(in chest behind illusory wall)
There are no upgrade materials in this location.
Behind the altar at theCathedral of the Forsakenis a hidden path, which reveals a labyrinth full of frenzied corpses and musically-inclined enemies. Three beams cross a pit with treacherous tombstone platforms sticking out from the walls. TheNomadic Merchant's Set,Eye of YeloughandNote: Miquella's Needleare inside three tents. They can only be reached by getting one of the frenziedNomadsto destroy them, or by standing right next to them, then quitting and reloading the game.
The alcove at one end of the middle beam has a Golden Rune (11), and the alcove at the end of the lowest beam has theFrenzied's Cookbook (2).
There is also a corpse with theInescapable Frenzyincantation, and a treasure chest at the lowest floor before the bottom with aFingerprint Stone Shieldat the end of a hallway. Once you have collected everything, jump to the bottom of the pit; the ground will collapse beneath you, leaving you next to the Frenzied Flame Proscription Site of Grace.
Hyettais also here, if you've progressed her questline to its conclusion. If you seek an audience with theThree Fingers, unequip all your armor and proceed to the locked door.This action will lock you into the Lord of Chaos ending unless remedied usingMiquella's Needle. You can then return to Hyetta who will speak of the objectives of the Three Fingers. Exhaust her dialogue, reload the area and collect theFrenzied Flame Sealwhere she once stood.
On the opposite wall from the Site of Grace, in the middle arch, is an illusory wall that will lead you to a chest containing aRune Arc. Behind this chest is another illusory wall that leads to the Root-Facing Cliffs Site of Grace inDeeproot Depths.
This is one of the few locations with no enemies or bosses. It is simply a room with a corridor and a door to the Three Fingers.

name: Miquella's Needle | Elden Ring Wiki
Miquella's Needleis aKey IteminElden Ring.Key ItemsinElden Ringinclude a wide variety of items found in specific locations or are given by a relatedNPCswhich are used to unlock areas, quests, and to further progress the game's story.
One of the unalloyed gold needles that Miquella crafted to ward away the meddling of outer gods.
Capable of subduing the flame of frenzy if inherited, allowing one to cheat fate and avoid becoming Lord of Frenzied Flame.
However, the needle is as yet unfinished and can only be used in the heart of the storm beyond time said to be found in FarumAzula.
Miquella's Needleis obtained after reaching one of the two possible conclusions toMillicent'squestline, and returning theUnalloyed Gold Needleto the Scarlet Aeonia left afterMalenia, Blade of Miquella'sfight.
Miquella's Needleis used atDragonlord Placidusax'sarena atCrumbling Farum Azulato reverse theThree Fingers' flame of frenzy. This is the only way to undo the Lord of Frenzied Flameending. To use it, simply select it from your inventory anywhere in the arena. Fighting Placidusax is NOT necessary to use the needle, simply being at the boss arena will do. The Dragon's area can also be accessed after defeated, so players can access the area even if they kill it to use the needle
Using this item to subdue the Flame of Frenzy will remove the yellow glow in your character's eyes gained by accepting the Frenzied Flame, but it will not undo the burn marks left on your characters body. (If youdowant to remove the burn marks for fashion purposes, you can easily do so by interacting with the mirror inFia's room in the Roundtable Hold, or by talking toRennalaafter defeating her and selecting the "Cosmetics" option.)
You can store up to 600Miquella's Needle.
Miquella's Needleis aTool IteminElden Ring.
This item is part ofMillicent's questline.
However, the needle is as yet unfinished and can only be used in the heart of the storm beyond time said to be found in Farum Azula.
Area: after completeling Millicent's questline by assisting her against her sisters to retrieve theUnalloyed Gold Needle, defeatMalenia, Blade of Miquellaand, upon reloading the area, interact with the Scarlet Aeonia flower.
This item can only be used within the arena ofDragonlord PlacidusaxinCrumbling Farum Azula: dispells the Flame of Frenzy inherited from theThree Fingersin the depths ofLeyndell, allowing to attain a different ending from theLord of Frenzied Flamefinale.
OnceMiquella's Needleis used, the burn marks from theThree Fingerswill remain, however theFrenzied Flameeye variation will be removed. The burn marks may be removed byRennaladuring character customization, it may also be reapplied at any time.

name: Destined Death | Elden Ring Wiki
Destined Deathis aSkillinElden Ring.Destined Deathallows the user to create a myriad of ethereal blade attacks to deal damage and inflicts a penalizing debuff onto enemies. Updated toPatch 1.07.
This Skill cannot beParriedThis Skill can beParriedif performed with no Focus
This Skill can beParriedif performed with no Focus
When triggered, the weapon art causes the user to do a right-to-left horizontal slash (hitbox 1), after which the blade is stabbed into the ground (hitbox 2), which then releases the blade vortex after a brief delay (hitbox 3).
Reduces enemy max HP by 10% for 45 seconds.
Damage scales with weapon AR and deals split physical and holy damage. The amount of physical and holy damage depends on stat investment, with Faith increasing Holy damage and Strength and Dexterity increasing physical damage.
The debuff stacks with theBlack Bladeincantation but not theBlade of Deathweapon skill.SeeBuffs and Debuffsfor more information on stacking debuffs.
Destined Death does triggerWinged Sword Insignia,Rotten Winged Sword Insignia,Millicent's ProsthesisandThorny Cracked Tear.
Note:This Skill was changed withPatch 1.07as follows:
Duration of the effect that reduces maximum HP has been extended.
Updated to patch1.07. SeePatch Notesfor details.
Formerly calledDestined Death Unboundin the 1.00 version.
