TheFormless Mother(姿なき母,Sugata-naki Haha), also known asMother of Truth(真実の母,Shinjitsu no Haha),[1]is an unseen character inELDEN RING(2022).
The Formless Mother is anOuter Godwho was encountered byMohgdeep underground. She is known to crave wounds, and to bestow power upon accursed blood.[2]Her body can be pierced usingMohgwyn's Sacred Spear, causing the weapon to become coated in Bloodflame, or an arm can be thrust into her body in order to scatter Bloodflame on the ground, using the incantationBloodboon.
Long ago, the Formless Mother was discovered by a subjugated tribe in the ravages of war, and were subsequently transformed intoBloodfiends.[3][4]Much like Mohg, the Bloodfiends made use of asacred spearto commune with the Formless Mother.[5]A delicacy of the bloodfiends, the blood fromSacred Bloody Fleshis said to have fallen from the Formless Mother's wound. Never will it dry, never will it rot.[6]

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Messmer the Impaler
Those stripped of theGrace of Goldshall all meet death. In the embrace ofMessmer's flame.
Messmer the Impaleris a mandatorybossinShadow of the Erdtree. He is aDemigodwho is encountered in theShadow Keep.
Messmer was a son ofQueen Marika the Eternal. He was born with a dark serpent inside him that threatened to subsume him, which Messmer has called theAbyssal Serpent; Marika was able to contain its influence by removing one of Messmer's eyes and replacing it with asealofgrace. Ever since his accursed birth, Messmer was in constant company of thewinged serpents.[1]
Much like hisyounger sister, Messmer bore a vision offire.[2]He despised thisflame, and time and time again hoped to rid himself of it, but found that it ever burned.[3]
At some point, Messmer befriendedCommander Gaius, anAlbinauricwho like him was cursed from birth. Gaius would go on to commandMessmer's armiesin the wars to come. They both acted as "older brothers" toGeneral Radahn.[4]
Before theShattering, Messmer was charged by his mother with carrying out a purge of thetower-dwellinghornsentof theLand of Shadow, who did not bear the light of grace. At some point during hisCrusade, Messmer was abandoned in theLand of Shadow, but continued to zealously enforce the purge even though Marika ceased all contact with him. Messmer came to reside in a fort known as theShadow Keep.
Key in his army were theBlack Knights, commanded byBlack Knight Commander Andreasand his son and second-in-commandBlack Knight Captain Huw. Although they remained devoutly loyal to Messmer despite his abandonment by Marika, they ultimately rebelled upon learning of hisserpentinenature. The pair were imprisoned in anunderground tomb, and despite his betrayal, Messmer mourned the loss of Huw, whom he had considered a brother-in-arms.[5][6]HisFire Knightsrebelled against burning theAncient Ruins of Rauhand the destruction of the specimens in theSpecimen Storehouse.[7][8]
Eventually, an intruder invaded Messmer's stronghold, the Shadow Keep, and was noticed by the demigod's serpents, who identified them asa Tarnished Championand a pretender to the title ofElden Lord. Though surprised that a Tarnished had come to the Land of Shadow, Messmer nonetheless attacked them to continue enforcing the purge. However, the serpentine demigod struggled overcome the Tarnished. Unwilling to accept "a Lord devoid of light" and desperate to regain the upper hand, Messmer ripped out Marika's seal and unleashed the power of the Abyssal Serpent, allowing him to frequently transform into a massive serpent. Nonetheless, the Tarnished was able to land a fatal blow upon Messmer. Realizing that his mother had indeed forsaken him, Messmer used his dying breath to curse Marika.
Messmer isnotan optional boss as he must be defeated in order to acquireMessmer's Kindlingthat would allow the burning of the Sealing Tree.
Hornsentcan be summoned for this boss. His summon sign is found inside of the boss room, and will appear if the player decides to side with him against Leda or ignore this part of Leda's quest.
Messmer's attacks are imbued with fire damage, making him a formidable opponent who relies heavily on his spear's reach and agility. To proceed in this boss fight, readiness for his swift movements is important. When fighting Messmer at a close range, you will have more chances of retaliating and chipping away at his health while he recovers. Engaging Messmer patiently is the best strategy to effectively take him down. When he finishes a string of attacks, focus on breaking his poise by pulling off heavy attacks for a chance to deal significant damage.
Because of his speed, Messmer can quickly transition between offense and defense by quickly disengaging with a leap after he finishes a move. Be aware that Messmer counters swiftly after sustaining damage, too. As his speed and precision in combat are his biggest asset, observation is required to avoid being overwhelmed. Once Messmer's health is half-depleted, a cutscene will trigger, which will start Messmer's second phase.
During the second phase, Messmer remains at 50% and not only retains his original attacks, but also introduces a set of new and more lethal attacks with the help of the Abyssal Serpent. Among the fresh additions to his move set is the ability to transform into a big red serpent that rises up to the ground to throw a fireball or do bite attacks. He also suffers a major weakness to Holy damage, likely a result of embracing the Abyssal Serpent that her mother sealed away in his eye.

area: Limgrave

name: Remembrance of the Grafted | Elden Ring Wiki
Remembrance of the Graftedis aConsumable IteminElden Ring. MostConsumablesgrant various effects such as restorative properties for recovering HP, removing certain negative status effects or applying temporary buffs and debuffs, while others can be thrown at enemies to deal damage.
Remembrance of Godrick, the Grafted, hewn into the Erdtree.
The power of its namesake can be unlocked by the Finger Reader.Alternatively, it can be used to gain a great bounty of runes.
A feeble man sought power through the grotesque act of grafting. "One day we'll return together, to our home, bathed in rays of gold."
Obtained as a reward for defeatingGodrick the GraftedatStormveil Castle. [Map Link] [Video Location]
Remembrance of the Graftedcan either be sold or consumed for 20,000Runes, or handed toEniainRoundtable Holdto unlock its power.

You can store up to 600Remembrance of the Grafted.

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Torrent (Spirit Steed) | Elden Ring Wiki
Torrent the Spectral Steedis a mount inElden Ring. Gifted to the Tarnished byMelinaearly in the game, he will be your constant companion, used for travel, exploration, and combat. This horned horse is summoned using theSpectral Steed Whistleand is highly agile, possessing a unique double jump ability that allows players to scale steep terrain and utilize Spiritsprings to reach otherwise inaccessible heights.
While invaluable in the open world, Torrent cannot be ridden within dungeons, nor can he be called upon duringPvPorCo-opsessions. It is also important to note that Torrent has his own health pool. He can be healed on the go by feeding him items like Rowa Raisins, but if he is killed in battle, players must consume one charge of the Flask of Crimson Tears to revive him.
To unlockTorrentinElden Ring, speak toMelinaat theGatefront RuinsSite of Grace. Agree to have her act as your maiden, and she will give you theSpectral Steed Whistlewhich you can use to summonTorrent. Put the whistle in your quick items or your pouch for easy access, since you'll be using it frequently!
Torrent can run faster and jump further than you can on foot, and learning to ride him effectively will make your time in the Lands Between much easier.
Torrent's normal walking speed is about as fast as your running speed on foot, and repeatedly dashing will double your speed again. Although Torrent's dash doesn't provide any invulnerability frames, it's fast enough to outpace almost any enemy, especially if they're winding up an attack.
Torrent's jumps go further than yours, but his most potent power is the ability to double-jump. This allows you to reach areas that would otherwise be totally inaccessible and even jump over some attacks. You can also change direction as you double-jump, which makes it the quickest way to turn Torrent around while running as well.
Attacks on horseback differ from those on foot. You can only hold one weapon at once, although you can switch between your right- and left-hand weapon. You can'ttwo-handa weapon either, so avoid using weapons whoseStrengthrequirements you can only meet while two-handing.
Each attack has a left- and right-side counterpart, which determines which side of Torrent you swing your weapon on. The light attacks are simple swings of your weapon, while the drag attacks can be held to drag your weapon along the ground, releasing it with a powerful swing. Although the timing is tricky, this is an excellent way to approach an enemy. Larger weapons' drag attacks can even launch foes into the air!
If you're wielding aSacred Sealor aGlintstone Staff, you'll cast a spell instead of doing your right light attack. If you're wielding aLight Bow,Bow, orCrossbow, you'll use the normal control scheme for that weapon instead, with the exception that you still can't use itsSkill.Shields,Greatbows, andBallistasare ineffective on horseback, and act as melee weapons instead.
You can do battle while riding Torrent, and in many cases this may be easier than fighting on foot. Torrent's speed makes it easy to outmaneuver most foes or quickly back off to safely heal or attack at range. He also has a hefty health bar of his own, and incoming attacks that are lower to the ground may hit him and leave you unscathed.
There are some situations in which mounted combat isn't the best option, though. In enclosed spaces, Torrent's speed can be more of a hindrance than a benefit, especially given how long it takes him to turn around. Torrent also has aStancebar of his own that repeated attacks can quickly fill, causing you to fall off. If this happens, it'll take a long time for you to get back on your feet, and you'll be vulnerable to attacks until then. Enemies wieldingTorchpolesare particularly problematic on horseback, since each attack connects multiple times from a relatively long distance.
If Torrent takes damage (or if you just want to give your good boy a treat), he can be healed withRowa Raisins,Sweet Raisins,Frozen Raisins, and theFlask of Crimson Tears. If Torrent dies, you will fall off and be stunned for multiple seconds. You can still summon Torrent even after he dies, but doing so costs a charge from the Flask of Crimson Tears and requires navigating a confirmation dialog. (If Torrent was merely stance-broken, he can be resummoned at no cost.)
Against larger enemies with slower attacks: Ride in, get in a few hits, and dash back out before you take damage. Because mounted attacks have a short delay, it's a good idea to start attacking as you approach the enemy. After the attack lands, continue past the enemy, using a dash or two if necessary to avoid an attack. Once you're clear, turn around, wait for your stamina to recover, and repeat. Getting distance is essential, since you can neitherdodgenorguardon horseback.
Against hordes of weaker enemies: Stay outside the group and use your Drag Attack to hit multiple enemies at a time. If you get caught in the middle, you'll quickly be knocked off.
Against ranged enemies: Lock on and spiral in towards them so you can get closer while dodging their projectiles.
Against enemies with faster attacks: Get in close as safely as you can and hit them repeatedly to keep them staggered. If you can't kill them with a single stamina bar, make sure to save some to ride away to safety.
During your journeys through the Lands Between you'll come across large, twister-like columns that are constantly spinning in place. These areSpiritsprings. You can jump into a Spiritspring while on horseback to ride its current high into the air and land safely nearby. Even if you jump down from a great height, landing near a Spiritspring will ensure you take no fall damage. They're often found near high cliffs and make it easy to pass between areas that differ greatly in altitude.
After acquiring Torrent, players can return to theChurch of EllehinLimgraveand rest at the site of grace to be given theSpirit Calling Bellby the witchRenna.
When using a crossbow while galloping on horseback, the player can fire their crossbow while in mid-air without unloading the crossbow as firing it normally would, allowing the player to fire their crossbow a second time immediately upon landing, without needing to reload (the Pulley Crossbow is excluded). This behavior is similar to the rapid follow-up shot the a player can achieve with a shortbow after jumping and firing it, albeit with stricter requirements.
When given theSpirit Calling Bellby the witchRenna, she mentions that it was entrusted to you by "Torrent's former master". The promotional material forShadow of the Erdtreeshows the EmpyreanMiquellaatop a horse similar to Torrent in theRealm of Shadow, hinting that perhaps there may be a connection.
Torrentis a spectral steed and the player's mount inELDEN RING(2022).
Torrent is a spectral steed resembling a horse with two short horns on his head and a white mane. Prior to meeting theTarnished, he is in the company ofMelina. The pair find the Tarnished unconscious in theStranded Graveyard, where Melina reassures Torrent[1]before granting the Tarnished two flasks. Later, when the Tarnished enters into an accord with Melina, she grants them theSpectral Steed Whistlewhich allows them to call upon Torrent, revealing that Torrent has chosen them.[2]
Torrent has a taste forRowa Raisins,[3]Sweet Raisins[4]andFrozen Raisins,[5]which can be used to restore his health. He had a former master who also gaveRanni the WitchtheSpirit Calling Bellto pass onto his next master.[6]The identity of this individual is not currently known.
Should the Tarnished choose to become the Lord of Frenzied Flame and incinerate theErdtree, a final cutscene will show Melina picking up the Spectral Steed Whistle, which disintegrates in her hand (though the player still has access to it in-game).
The player can acquire Torrent fromMelinaat any time by either resting at theGatefront RuinsorAgheel Lake Northsites of graceor after touching three different sites of grace then resting at any of the additional graces:
Besides allowing a player to get around relatively quickly, Torrent also doesn't appear to take fall damage from certain heights. This allows one to easily jump down from heights that'd normally kill the player as long as they're mounted on Torrent. That said, Torrent isn't immune to dying from jumping from too high of a height: even if a double jump is used to get to a lower level, if the starting point is too high up, Torrent will dissipate on landing and the player will die from the impact.
Jumping again while in mid-air will cause Torrent to perform a second jump. This can only be done once until he touches the ground again and can be used to change direction at the moment of the second jump.
Players can also fight from horseback against enemies, such as shooting arrows or casting spells. However, only one of the player's weapons can be used at a time as the left hand is constantly occupied holding Torrent's reigns, it is still possible to switch between the right-hand and left-hand armament while riding by using the same input the player uses to two-hand their weapons.
Note that it is not possible to change from wielding a weapon one-handed to two-handed while mounted. It is however possible to get the bonuses of two-handing by performing the action before mounting up.
Spirit springs can be used by jumping while riding Torrent to reach higher altitudes. Landing on or close to a spirit spring will completely negate fall damage.
Torrent's HP can be restored by consumingRowa Raisins,Sweet RaisinsandFrozen Raisins. Using aFlask of Crimson Tearswill also restore his health on top of the player's own, however only while the player is riding him. If Torrent is killed, using the Spectral Steed Whistle will bring up a prompt to expend a single charge of the Flask of Crimson Tears to revive him.

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Divine Towers
TheDivine Towersare six mysterious spires in theLands Between. They serve as the locations at which theTarnishedcan activate the power of theGreat Runesof theElden Ring.
Most of the Divine Towers are connected to the land by the Divine Bridges. They form a near-equilateral hexagon around the inner sea of the Lands Between. The towers themselves are octagonal in shape, built into massive spires of rock. They are decorated with insets of meteorite with seats ofTwo Fingersat the top.
The towers are ancient; an in-game painting indicates that the Divine Tower in Limgrave predates the construction ofStormveil Castle- in fact, it was already falling to ruin before any evidence of the castle's creation.[1]

name: Divine Tower of Limgrave Walkthrough and Items | Elden Ring Wiki
Divine Tower of Limgraveis aLocationinElden Ring. TheDivine Tower of Limgraveis one of the six Divine Towers found throughout the Lands Between. Located east of Stormveil Castle, this tower serves as the site where players can restore the power ofGodrick's Great Runeafter defeatingGodrick the Grafted.
Divine Tower of Limgrave Map in Elden Ring
All Items in the Divine Tower of Limgrave in Elden Ring
Enemies and Bosses in the Divine Tower of Limgrave in Elden Ring
Divine Tower of Limgrave Full Walkthrough in Elden Ring
Stormhawk Feather- run backwards out of the tower
Can unlockGodrick's Great Runeby channeling at the top of the tower.
This is the location where you can restoreGodrick's Great Runeto full strength and have it grant you its power. To reach the location, take the long bridge east ofStormveil Castlefrom the Limgrave Tower Bridge Site of Grace.  Many players won't have this Site of Grace initially, as it requires you to have navigated the ballistae gauntlet from Stormveil Main Gate or from having navigated most of Stormveil Castle and approaching from the opposite direction.
Some tips, if coming from the Stormveil Main Gate Site of Grace:
Summoning just as you enter the area is helpful, as it will provide additional targets for the ballistae
Run forward about 50 yards until there is an opening to the right
Sprint for the large open arch, but beware: a tough enemy will try to stop you
Once through, the Limgrave Tower Bridge Site of Grace is a short sprint away!
You can loot theBoltdrake Talismanfrom a body ascending the stairs toward the tower. This leads to a long Stormhill bridge covered withGiant Golems. You can choose to fight them or run through them. Killing the Giant Archers will give you a chance to gain theGolem Greatbow. Before using the waygate, you can safely drop down behind the ledge to find aSoft Cottonand theAsh-of-War Scarabhelm.
Interact with the waygate at the end of the bridge to reach the other side. This will take you to the front steps of the Divine Tower of Limgrave. Step to the center to activate the lift. Continue forward, and there will be anotherSite of Grace. Continue heading up the stairs and you'll eventually reach a site where you can restore the power of the Great Rune. This is only available after defeatingGodrick the GraftedatStormveil Castle. You will then obtainGodrick's Great Rune. You must have defeatedGodrick; otherwise, the gate of the tower will be locked.
Notes and Tips for theDivine Tower of LimgraveLocationinElden Ringgo here.
There is a Two Fingers on a mound of earth at the top of this tower, in the centre of eight meteorite fragments.
The door entering this divine tower faces east-northeast, and the entrance to the top faces north-northwest, an angle of ninety degrees from entering the tower. The tower is covered with what appears to be molten rock on its north face.
Divine Tower of Limgraveis a location inELDEN RING(2022).
The Divine Tower of Limgrave rises out of the sea to the north of Limgrave, connected toStormveil Castleby a great bridge which has crumbled in the middle and can only be traversed through the use of a Sending Gate.
A trio ofGuardian Golemsawait on the bridge; two wield  axes while a third fires giant arrows on approach.
Once the player has claimedGodrick's Great Rune, they may restore its power at the top of the tower, by interacting with the glowing Rune in front of the corpse of aTwo Fingers.

area: Limgrave

name: Divine Tower of Liurnia | Elden Ring Wiki
Divine Tower of Liurniais aLocationinElden Ring. It is one of the sixDivine Towers. TheDivine Tower of Liurniais found inLiurnia of the Lakesand is reached by taking the lift down at the secret area ofCarian Study Hall.
TheDivine Tower of Liurniacan only be accessed by inverting theCarian Study Hallusing theCarian Inverted Statue. This statue is acquired by progressingRanni'squestline up to the point where you hand her theFingerslayer Blade.
Once inverted, players need to reach the lift in the center of the Study Hall by careful platforming and then go through the large doors after descending the lift. This leads to the long bridge to the tower. Beware of theGodskin Nobleenemy guarding the center of the bridge. [Elden Ring Map here]
There are no regular enemies in this location
TheGodskin Noblefought at the bridge drops the entireGodskin Noble Setupon defeat. The tower itself is a fairly straightforward affair. Through the main doors, ascend the lift and then follow the path along the balconies, grabbing the Divine Tower Of Liurnia site of grace on the way. At the top of the tower, you can loot theStargazer Heirloomtalisman andCursemark of Deathkey item from the corpse on the ground.
Divine Tower of Liurniais a location inELDEN RING(2022).
The Divine Tower of Liurnia stands on a rocky outcropping off the eastern coast ofLiurnia of the Lakes, accessed via theCarian Study Hall. Unlike every other Divine Tower, there is no Great Rune to restore here. Instead, the player will find the corpse ofRanni the Witch, bearing the evidence of her involvement in theNight of Black Knives.

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Divine Tower of Caelid | Elden Ring Wiki
Divine Tower of Caelidis aLocationinElden Ring. It is one of the sixDivine Towers. TheDivine Tower of Caelidis found inDragonbarrow. Players can reach this location by heading northeast from the Dragonbarrow West Site of Grace (or the closer Isolated Merchant in Calid). This tower cannot be accessed by conventional methods and will require careful platforming starting from the roots that extend from the Dragonbarrow plateau towards the tower's sides and using the ledges and ladders along the side of the tower.
There are no NPCs or Merchants at this location
Godskin Apostle Bracelets(Godskin Apostle drop)
Godskin Apostle Hood(Godskin Apostle drop)
Godskin Apostle Robe(Godskin Apostle drop)
Godskin Apostle Trousers(Godskin Apostle drop)
This tower is best visited after defeatingStarscourge Radahnand acquiring his Great Rune.
To get into the tower, summonTorrentand ride off towards the tower in the northeast from the Dragonbarrow West Site of Grace. On the way, you can find a Teardrop Scarab on a dead tree root protruding out of the ground, kill it to get aSomber Smithing Stone [8]; be mindful that this scarab will explode on death, so dodge out of the way after. Continue northeast.
At the edge of the plateau, you will see a large root protruding from the cliffs towards the tower. Jump onto this root and follow it high enough till you can safely jump towards one of the tower's ledges to the left. Beware of the soldier on this ledge and take him out carefully. Note there are a couple of paths to choose & items that can be collected ahead. You can still summon Torrent, whose double jump you can use to aid in the platforming.
Traverse right from the bottom of the first ladder: Climb over one curved ledge and kill one soldier to pick up aStonesword Key.
Traverse left from the bottom of the first ladder: Climb over one curved ledge. Beware the crack at the left end of it. You are now between two ladders. Climbing up is a dead end. With some careful double jumping, you can probably get around the statues, but there aren't items to obtain. Head down to the bottom of the bottom ladder and kill the foot soldier. Around to the left and right are both dead ends with no items.
Take the ladder up and traverse right: Pass over two triangular ledges. There's a crack at the end of both of them you must jump over. You can jump down towards theStonesword Keymentioned above, or go back the way you came.
Take the ladder up and traverse left: This is the way forward. Jump over the two cracks on the triangular ledge. You are now on the ledge above the pair of ladders. Go around the corner and kill the foot soldier. Jump across the next triangular ledge, avoiding the two cracks on the right and third on the left. Go past the ladder to find a corpse with aNumen's Rune. Return to the previous ladder and climb up to find theDivine Tower of Caelid: Centergrace site. Or proceed directly to the site of grace, and get the Numen's Rune later.
Head west from the Site of Grace and up the steps to find the door towards the main tower lift. Note that the door is on theleftside of the corridor and can easily be mistaken by the engravings on the center wall. Step on the platform in the middle to ascend the lift and then follow the steps around the balconies to reach the top floor and restore power toRadahn's Great Rune.
There is a boss to be found at the base of the tower. To reach this location, head east from the Center Site of Grace and down the steps. You will encounter twoRadahn Soldiershere and a locked door at the end. Look down below to the right to find a long concrete platform you can jump down to. Look behind you and you will find narrow ledges along the walls that you can walk on. Walk towards a second concrete platform on the left and jump on it. It will break and come crashing down a few levels below but don't worry, you will not suffer fall damage from this.
Walk over to the thinner portion that the platform crashed on and carefully drop down to the wider platform below. There is a corpse here with aGolden Rune (12). Walk towards the center of the platform and look down at the right (north) side to find an unlit lamp sticking out the tower's center. Carefully jump onto this lamp and then onto the concrete platform below. Jump onto the half-beam next to you and then down the two half-beams ahead and below that one. You should now be closer to the tower's center with a soldier to your left. Take him out with ranged attacks if possible and then head to where he was and ride the cage elevator up.
You will arrive on a balcony with a long ladder to the right. This ladder leads up to a room where you can unlock the door from earlier to gain a shortcut in case you die in the next section. Head back down the ladder and continue along the corridor to find aBlackflame Monkpatrolling the hallway. Be careful as his spells are very powerful and he is quite nimble with his blade as well. After defeating the monk, check the corpse at the end of the corridor for aRune Arc.Do not jump down to the beam that leads towards the centre, as that will loop you back to the elevator you just took.
At the corpse looking at the main column, look to the right of the inner tower and note the concrete platform that has cracks in it like the previous one you rode in on, albeit nervously. Get up on the ledge by the corpse and run along the outer wall. Follow it to the placement of the concrete platform below that you can jump on. This one will come crashing down as well but again, you will not suffer fall damage despite the very long fall. There is another cage elevator here that will take you to the basement. You can find the Basement Site of Grace after descending the lift. From here, head down the steps to fight another monk and you will have arrived at the boss door.
The Godskin Apostle is a powerful boss equipped with a twinblade that has a sickle-end for slashing and a blade-end for thrusting and stabbing. He utilizes Black Flame spells similar to the monks earlier in the tower. When fighting this boss, you want to maintain a medium distance to avoid many of his attacks and only close in during openings. His melee attacks have a bit of weight to them and he does short wind-ups before attacking, similar to but not to the same extent as Margit at Stormveil.
Some notable attack windows are when he performs his Stab & Slash; he has a moderate recovery time after the second attack in which you can safely get one or two hits in. Another one is his Jumping Overhead Slash which has a slightly longer recovery than other attacks and can guarantee 2 hits for you. These two attacks are relatively easy to dodge. The attacks you should watch out for are his Black Flame as it travels quite quickly, you should dodge as soon as you see the casting rune; and his Stab & Pull which hits twice for massive damage. Another move he may use is the Spinning Weapon in which he twirls his blade in front of him as he advances forward. Maintain your distance or dodge through and behind him.
Picture of the Caelid Divine Tower, as seen from Dragonbarrow Fork, showing the molten rock on its east side.
Divine Tower of Caelidis a location inELDEN RING(2022).
A Divine Tower in the northern section ofGreyoll's DragonbarrowinCaelid. The Divine Tower of Caelid is unique among Divine Towers, as the only way to access it is to scale the outside, making use of narrow platforms and ladders. In addition, the interior of the Divine Tower can also be explored once the player has ascended to the mid-point.
At the top of the tower, the player may restore power toRadahn's Great Runeby interacting with the glowing Rune in front of the corpse of aTwo Fingers.

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Divine Tower of West Altus | Elden Ring Wiki
Divine Tower of West Altusis aLocationinElden Ring. It is one of the sixDivine Towers. TheDivine Tower of West Altusis found inCapital OutskirtsbetweenAltus PlateauandLeyndell, Royal Capital. It can only be reached by going through a series of illusory walls found inSealed Tunnel. The path is linear, so there's no way to miss it, and illusory walls are generally at the end of each new area. You have to fightOnyx Lordwhich can be defeated in your first encounter if you are prudent enough.
NOTE:You cannot access the Divine Tower of West Altus without first defeatingRykard, Lord of Blasphemy. Otherwise, you'll get a message saying the "[The door] is tightly blocked shut"
Interactive Map Location here. [Elden Ring Map here]
There are no NPCs or Merchants in this location
There are no gatherables in this location.
There are no Enemies within this location
Reach this tower after defeatingRykard, Lord of Blasphemyat theVolcano Manorand obtainingRykard's Great Rune[Elden Ring Map Link] to restore its power. Choose to reach this location before this event and you will instead be greeted with itstightly blocked shutdoors.
The entrance to theDivine Toweris hidden and can only be found by going through a series of illusory walls and defeatOnyx Lordin theSealed Tunnel. (Follow theSealed TunnelGuide to reach this area.)
Once you reach the tower, step to the center of the tower platform to ascend. Take the stairs all the way up wrapping around the exterior of the tower to eventually reach. Here, you can restore the power of the Great Rune.
TheDivine Tower of Limgrave(left) and theDivine Tower of Liurnia(right) as seen from theDivine Tower of West Altus.
Divine Tower of West Altusis a location inELDEN RING(2022).
A Divine Tower south-west ofLeyndell, Royal Capital. It can only be accessed by passing through theSealed Tunnel.
At the top of the tower, the player may restore power toRykard's Great Runeby interacting with a glowing Rune in front of the corpse of aTwo Fingers

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Divine Tower of East Altus | Elden Ring Wiki
Divine Tower of East Altusis aLocationinElden Ring. It is one of the sixDivine Towers. TheDivine Tower of East Altusis found inCapital Outskirts. Found at the very east of theLeyndell, Royal Capitalregion.
No NPCs can be found in the vicinity of this location.
Start at central Leyndell’s Avenue Balcony site of grace, then go up the stairs and turn left.  Follow the road to the large door out of the central city.  Go out the door and up the stairs in the ashy sandy area past a vicious mob.  Follow the path and a door to the left will hold a wooden court-room style elevator.   The route after the elevator leads both to another elevator to theForbidden Landsor also to a different southeast exit with a lone Leyndell Soldier patrolling a path - approach him and you'll be ambushed by theFell Twins. After you defeat them and reap the rewards of this battle, the way forward leads to the Divine Tower.
If you already have the Forbidden Lands grace unlocked, then just warp there, go up the elevator, and leave the elevator tower by the southern exit.
This is the only Divine Tower where you can activate two Great Runes - Morgott's and Mohg's.
There is a Two Fingers on a mound of earth at the top of this tower, in the centre of eight meteorite fragments.
The door entering this divine tower faces south-southeast and the entrance to the top faces east-northeast, an angle of 90 degrees off entering the tower. The tower is covered with what appears to be molten rock on its east-northeast face (to the left as you enter it).
Divine Tower of East Altusis a location inELDEN RING(2022).
A Divine Tower south-east ofLeyndell, Royal Capital, connected to the city via a greatbridge. When crossing the bridge, the player will be transported to a pitch black space and accosted by theFell Twins. After defeating them, the player will find themselves at the gate to the tower.
Morgott's Great RuneandMohg's Great Runecan both be restored at the top of this tower, by interacting with the corresponding Rune in front of the corpse of aTwo Fingers.

name: Isolated Divine Tower | Elden Ring Wiki
Isolated Divine Toweris aLocationinElden Ring. It is one of the sixDivine Towers. TheIsolated Divine Towercan be reached by taking the waygate from the Divine Bridge inLeyndell Royal Capital. [Map Link] Reaching this Site of Grace can be done in two ways, via the chest found atTower of Returnor through the Fortified Manor in the capital by going through a closed door in the main hall and taking the elevator. After defeating Maliketh, the only way is through the Tower of Return which can be found to the southwest in theWeeping Peninsula.
Ascend the tower to restoreMalenia's Great Rune.
Like all Divine Towers, the respective shardbearer,Malenia, must be killed before the doors can be opened.
This is one of the few areas whereFarum Azulais visible from far away.
TheIsolated Divine Toweras seen from theBestial Sanctum.
Isolated Divine Toweris a location inELDEN RING(2022).
A Divine Tower to the far east of theLands Between, it is physically disconnected from the mainland and can only be reached by taking theSending Gatefrom theDivine Bridgelocated inLeyndell.
The Divine Bridge can be reached via a chest found at theTower of Return, or at theFortified Manorby entering a closed door in the main hall, then riding up an elevator. OnceMalikethhas been defeated, the Divine Bridge is only accessible through the Tower of Return.
At the top of the tower, the player may restore power toMalenia's Great Runeby interacting with a glowing Rune in front of the corpse of aTwo Fingers.

---

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: War Against the Giants
TheWar Against the Giantsrefers to the conflict between the Fire Giants and the champions of theErdtree, long before the events ofELDEN RING(2022).
Long ago, the red-haired Fire Giants took up residence in the northernMountaintops, chasing away the ice dragons who were the former lords of the region.[1]The Fire Giants were considered neighbors by the astrologers who had also established themselves on the mountaintops.[2]
The Giants borrowed a destructive, fiery power from a fell god, whose one-eyed visage[3]manifested upon their chests, however the cost for this was eternal servitude as keepers of the flame of ruin[4], which resided within the forge of the Giants.
Meanwhile,Queen Marika the Eternal, anEmpyreanvessel of theElden Ring, had begun to establish her reign over theLands Between. The flame of ruin posed a threat to the burgeoning Erdtree, being capable of burning it[5], and thus needed to be neutralized. And so, Queen Marika and her consortGodfrey, First Elden Lord, marched upon the Mountaintops of the Giants
The war against the Giants, fought at the birth of the Erdtree[6], was led by Godfrey.[7]They marched through the western Mountaintops, carving winding paths to the summit.[8]Upon arriving in the Mountaintops, Queen Marika issued a proclamation to Godfrey and his warriors, commanding them to put the Giants to the sword and confine their flame, so that the Age of the Erdtree could begin.[9]
The heroes of the Erdtree were accompanied by theFire Monks, who devised anincantationwhich could protect them from the Giants' flame.[10]They were also joined by theKnights of Zamor, who had been mortal enemies of the Fire Giants since time immemorial[11], having challenged them many times in the past.[12]
TheTrolls, who were descendants of the Giants[13], betrayed their ancestors[14]and fought on behalf of the Erdtree. They were furnished with gilded swords[15]to commemorate their fealty.
The Giants retaliated, using their bellowing roars to trigger avalanches and whip up storms of flame.[16]Facing a Fire Giant was seen as a horror, thanks in part to their dreadful visages and the flames they wielded.[17]Enormous, crushing weapons were deployed to counter their onslaught[18], and the heroes of the Erdtree strengthened their arms using semi-vitrified smithing stones found in the cold, northern regions.[6]
Queen Marika herself did battle with the one-eyed fell god, and it is believed to have been slain by her.[3]In truth, the fell god continued to lurk within the Fire Giants themselves.[19]Despite the odds, the champions of the Erdtree prevailed over the Fire Giants[4], leaving the battlefield littered with their corpses.
Although the Giants had been defeated, it became apparent that the flame of ruin would never die. Seeing this, Queen Marika marked a lone survivingFire Giantwith a curse, compelling him to tend to the flame for eternity.[20]With the flame sealed away, the Fire Monks andFlame Guardianswere appointed to watch over it.[21][22]They would later succumb to the allure of the flame[23], emblazoning their chestplates with depictions of the fell god.[24]
The Knights of Zamor earned great renown[25]for their actions during the war, and were hailed as heroes. They can be found in Hero's Graves, seemingly serving as guardians. The Trolls, despite their own efforts in the war, did not receive such recognition, and can often be found performing menial labour, working in mines or dragging carriages.
The end of the war marked the dawn of the era of the Erdtree[14], presided over by Queen Marika and Godfrey. The Erdtree itself would go on to become the embodiment of Order[26], its blessed sap dripping from its boughs. The age of plenty which ensued ended swiftly, however, and the Erdtree became more an object of faith.[27]
Although the flame of ruin was sealed, the burning of the Erdtree was considered to be the first cardinal sin[28]. Prophets would occasionally glimpse the flame of ruin in their faith, envisioning the ruin that it would bring.[29]Prophets who had such visions would be banished[30], forced to wear shackles around their necks to warn passersby against listening to them.[31]
Some time afterThe Shattering, aTarnishedwould arrive in the Lands Between and meetMelina, a mysterious woman who would guide them along the path to become Elden Lord. Finding that the entrance to the Erdtree was obstructed by thorns, Melina advises the Tarnished that the only way to gain entry was to set the Erdtree aflame.[32]The pair journey to the giant's forge, where the Tarnished fights and defeats the Fire Giant whom Marika had left to tend the Flame. Melina offers herself as kindling, and sets fire to the Erdtree using the fire that had long been sealed away.

---

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Carian Royal Family | Elden Ring Wiki
TheCarian Royal Familyis a powerful magic-basedfactioninElden Ring. Founded byRennala, Queen of the Full Moon, the Carian Royals lead theRaya Lucaria Academyand their study ofglintstone sorceries. Under their employ are select servants, soldiers, preceptors and a group of renowned knights. SeeCarian Sorceriesfor the related spell class.
The fate of the Carian royal family is guided by the stars. - War Counselor Iji
Queen Rennala was once an astrologer who studied the stars. She then came into contact with the full moon, and learned powerful magic that can absorb other spells, and this allowed her to eventually lead theRaya Lucaria Academy. She then founded the Carian royal house, with an order of sworn knights to protect it and servants such as preceptors to help guide it. Included in her ranks were trolls who wielded magic and were also treated asknights. At an indeterminate point, the First Liurnian War broke out between Raya Lucaria and the Golden Order ofLeyndell, Royal Capital. As aSword Monumentreads, Radagon of the Golden Order took part in this conflict. After the Second Liurnian War, from which no clear victor arose, atonement mended the relationship between Rennala and Radagon and the two were wed at theChurch of Vows, which brought an end to the conflict between Leyndell and Raya Lucaria. Rennala was not universally accepted at the academy, as many disliked seeing the moon as equal to the stars. According to theLazuli Robe, those outside the Lazuli Conspectus saw this robe in the hue of the full moon as a signifier of their heresy. Though being responsible for forbidding the study of thePrimeval Current, her use of the spellComet Azurlikely implies Rennala had some connection to it.
Lord Radagon was an enigmatic figure in the Lands Between. He despised his red locks for which he was known for, and which could have been a curse from the long since defeatedFire Giants. Radagon first gained recognition in the Liurnian Wars, and later usedCelestial Dewto reconcile with the Carian Queen Rennala of the Full Moon. After their reconciliation, Radagon wed Rennala and received a greatsword as a gift from her. Together they had three demigod children, Rykard, Radahn, and Ranni. When Radagon married Rennala, he ordered the Carian preceptors to don themask of confidence. To make it clear that all of their matters were to be kept strictly private. WhenGodfrey, First Elden Lorddefeated his last worthy foe, he was divested of grace and banished from the land along with his tarnished army. Radagon then left Rennala to return to Leyndell and become the second Elden Lord withQueen Marika. Before departing he left Rennala with anamber eggand his loyalred wolf. His children with Rennala became demigod stepchildren, and he had the Twin ProdigiesMiquellaandMaleniawith Queen Marika. As the husband of Rennala of Caria, the red-haired Radagon studiedsorcery, and as the husband of Queen Marika, he studiedincantations. Thus did the hero aspire to be complete. To symbolize the tenets of the Golden Order, Radagon reforged the greatsword given to him by Rennala into agreatsword of lightmodeled after the Elden Ring.
Rellana is the sister of Queen Rennala, and a Carian princess by birthright. They were close since childhood, and Rellana learned powerful sorcery fromCount Ymir. She was also a formidable fighter who at one point used theCarian Thrusting Shieldin ritual combat to show fidelity to the Erdtree. Those that followedMessmer'scrusade against theBelurat Tower, even knights hailing from renowned families of the Erdtree's upper echelons, were shunned and chased from their homes after pledging allegiance to Messmer. Among those that chased after Messmer included Rellana, who disavowed her birthright and chose to stand at Messmer's side instead. After some time she became known as the Sword of Messmer and received a straight sword engraved with golden flame. Carian knights who served as direct retainers to Carian princesses such as Rellana received aCarian Filigreed Crest. Then there were those who left their homelands to serve Rellana, recounted by theRellana's Cameotalisman; "By your leave, we will accompany you wherever your lunar vessel takes you." Before Rellana departed, Rennala was said to have given her younger sister a gift of lustrous black hair.
Rykard is the son of Queen Rennala and Radagon, and was adept at sorceries just like his mother. After discovering the ancient hexes ofMt. Gelmir, Rykard brought them back into practical use as new forms of sorcery. At some point Rykard struck out on his own and raised his own banners, becoming the figurehead of theVolcano Manor. This could be because Caria is a matriarchy, and according to War Counselor Iji, Lady Ranni is the first heir in the Carian royal line. Rykard and his inquisitors committed numerous atrocities so that he could wage war with Leyndell. At some point he met LadyTanith, a dancer from a foreign land, who became his consort at Volcano Manor. During the Shattering Rykard bore aGreat Rune, but fed it and himself to an ancient serpent. After this, the birth of theman-serpentssoon followed. Rykard was rewarded with atoolafter the Night of the Black Knives, which would allow him to challengeMaliketh, the Black Blade. Rykard would gather champions to the Volcano Manor to become recusants and hunt down the tarnished and rebel against the forces of the Erdtree. According to theTaker's Cameo, when Rykard turned to heresy, taking by force became the rule. To him the gods themselves were no different, after all.
Radahn is the son of Queen Rennala and Radagon, and has flowing red hair just like his father. Radahn was fond of his heritage, letting his hair poke out behind his helmet and taking the Redmane moniker for himself. According to Radahn; "I was born a champion's cub. Now I am the Lord of the Battlefield's lion." Inspired by heroes of the battlefield such as Godfrey, Serosh, and his father, he modeled his armor and likeness after them. At some point Radahn struck out on his own and raised his own banners, leading the Redmanes. This could be because Caria is a matriarchy, and according to War Counselor Iji, Lady Ranni is the first heir in the Carian royal line. Radahn learnt powerfulgravity sorceriesfrom anAlabaster LordinSellia, Town of Sorceryso that he could challenge the stars and continue to ride beloved but scrawny steed. After succeeding in locking the stars into place, he became known as the Starscourge. During the Shattering Radahn bore aGreat Runeand took part in many conflicts, ultimately fighting against Malenia in one final confrontation inCaelid. Now mindless from scarlet rot, he still roams the battlefield.
Ranni is the self-described daughter of Queen Rennala and Radagon, and a princess of Caria. Ranni was anEmpyreanchosen by the Two Fingers, and as such was a potential candidate to succeed Queen Marika and usher in a new age. Due to this she received Blaidd as a shadow-bound beast who would protect her, and along with Iji they have been together since childhood. Rennala imparted onto her powerful sorceries including her dark moon, which was veiled in occult mystery. Her true mentor though was a mysterious snow witch who taught hercold sorcery. Ranni came to despise her eventual fate of being controlled by the Two Fingers, and endeavored to free herself with the aid of her companions. She is the one predominately responsible for the Night of the Black Knives, stealing a fragment of the Rune of Death from Malekith and imbuing it onto a series ofdaggers, after which a group ofassassinsused them to killGodwyn the Goldenin spirit while Ranni herself discarded her flesh. According to theCursemark of Death, two demigods perished at the same time, breaking the cursemark into two half-wheels. Ranni was the first of the demigods whose flesh perished, while the Prince of Death perished in soul alone. Ranni then possessed a doll modeled after her mentor and returned to theCarian Manorwhere she had grown up, and continues to work in secret.
The Carian Knights were a group of magic-wielding knights sworn to the Carian Royal Family. According to theCarian Knight's Sword, these knights' swords could serve as catalysts, letting them wield sorcerous battle skills. Despite numbering fewer than twenty, this power made them a match for even the champions of gold in battle. Called into service when the Queen invoked an oath they swore, even trolls were in the ranks of the knights of Caria, and fought arm in arm with their human comrades. The enchanted knights, anointed by the Lunar Queen, were heroes of the highest honors, but fell into disarray with the decline of the royal family. The Raya Lucaria Academy turned on the Carians with the aid of theCuckoo Knights, and laid an unsuccessful siege on the Carian Manor. The Carians however knew of the academy's disloyalty, and developed theCarian Retaliationspell as a countermeasure. The moon and stars would one day go their separate ways.Notable members of the knights includedMoongrumwho guards Queen Rennala,Bolswho was captured by the Cuckoos,Moonrithyllwho was the Twin Moon Knight's chamberlain, andRoyal Knight Lorettawho was a former personal guard. Loretta left the Carian royals to seek out a place where the Albinaurics could live in peace, eventually finding the secretiveHaligtree.
Jerren is an old knight who once preferred a nomadic existence, but after spending time as a guest of the Carian royals, he became a guest commander for General Radahn. And for the first time, the restless tumbleweed would be bound by an honorable oath. This oath would be one of honorable death between him and Radahn while Jerren was in his service. At the end of the Shattering, when Malenia and Radahn battled in Caelid leading to aScarlet Aeoniathat devastated the land, General Radahn who was known as the strongest of the demigods did not perish there on the battlefield. Instead he was infected by thescarlet rot, becoming more animalistic and as Jerren describes, his wits are long gone. Wishing to give his old friend a proper death, Jerren plans to host a grand festival atCastle Redmane, gathering all the champions from across the land for a chance to slay Radahn and lay claim to his Great Rune. At the castle scarlet rot is kept at bay with flame, and as such, Jerren's belovedswordfeaturing a flame-like undulation eventually became the symbol of the castle itself. Jerren is also known as the Witch-Hunter, and Iji recounts that he made an old promise to hunt down the one known as theGraven Witch, that they may finally be rid of a longstanding Carian weed.
Blaidd is the stepbrother and sworn protector of Ranni, and possesses a large wolf-like appearance. He was gifted to Ranni by the Two Fingers, and according to Iji earned the approval of Queen Rennala. According to the old legends, wolves are the shadows of Empyrean which could explain some of Blaidd's features. Once there was an assassin who assumed the guise of Ranni the Witch's loyal shadow using ablack wolf mask. In defiance of the fate he was born to, Blaidd swore to serve no master but Ranni. As proof, theswordhe received was imbued with a cold magic at the moment the oath was sworn. Bothered by the cold, Blaidd wears a pelt fashioned as a cape. Iji warns that if Lady Ranni as an Empyrean continues to resist being an instrument of the Two Fingers, her shadow Blaidd will go mad, transforming from a follower into a horrid curse. But such is his destiny, and Blaidd would defy destiny itself if it would have him turn upon his Lady. Iji, who had long served the Carian Royals as a blacksmith, became Ranni's war counselor when she decided to turn against the Two Fingers. He wears amirrorhelmto protect against the Fingers' language of light as he is terribly frightened by his own treachery. It seems fear guides some of his actions, as he later imprisons Blaidd. He reflects on this mistake, hoping to meet Blaidd again and give him an apology.
Seluvis is a preceptor of the Carian Royals, similar toPreceptor Miriamin theCarian Study Hall. He is a teacher of the sorcerous arts and aids Ranni along with Blaidd and Iji, though Blaidd is not very fond of him. The movements of the stars are drawn inside the brim of his hat and on his gown, and he has a particular obsession withStarlight Shards. He can begrudgingly help find the pathway that leads to theEternal City of Nokronthrough his connection to the Sorceress Sellen. Notably, one of his puppetsTherolinaalso takes part in the festival at Castle Redmane to defeat General Radahn. Seluvis's secret lair can be discovered not far fromRanni's Rise, where he keeps a collection of puppets. By using a specialpotionSeluvis is able to fashion a puppet out of the person who drank the potion, which also leads to the death of said person. One of his victims includesDolores the Sleeping Arrow, who once belonged to theRoundtable Hold, where she was both a critic and a friend ofGideon the All-Knowing. It was because of her that he and Seluvis went their separate ways. Gideon holds a deep distain for Seluvis, referring to him as a twisted dolly botherer. Whether by coincidence, Seluvis has also taken an interest inNepheli Louxwho also has a connection to Sir Gideon. Pidia is a servant of the Carian Royal Family and resides at the Carian Manor. He is afirst-generation albinauric, and as such has gray skin and immobile legs. Albinaurics are lifeforms made by human hands. Thus, many believe them to live impure lives, untouched by the Erdtree's grace. He and Seluvis seem to work together since Pidia looks after some puppets and possesses a map that is part of Seluvis's plan. His plan involves betraying Princess Ranni, but Ranni may know this as she says "heed not their peculiarities; feel secure in gaining from them what advantage thou canst. I am sure the others will be doing just the same." After retrieving theFingerslayer Bladefor Ranni, Seluvis is found dead and Pidia is attacked by his own puppets. It could be inferred that Pidia puppeteered Seluvis from the start, and after their usefulness came to an end Ranni had them both killed.

When Rennala, head of both the Academy of Raya Lucaria and the Carian royal family, lost her husband Radagon, her heart went along with him.
And then, those at the academy realized. That Rennala was no champion, after all.
Greatsword made of light, modeled after the Elden Ring itself. Forged by King Consort Radagon to proudly symbolize the tenets of the Golden Order. One of the legendary armaments.
Telltale signs betray that this was once the greatsword bequeathed to him by his first wife, Rennala.
Ornate helm of Rellana, the Twin Moon Knight, fashioned from silver steel. Rennala, head of the royal family of Caria, was said to have given her younger sister, who renounced her lineage to chase after Messmer, a gift of lustrous black hair.
A Great Rune of the shardbearer Rykard. Its blessing restores HP on attacking enemies.
Rykard was amongst the children of Rennala and Radagon, who became demigod stepchildren after Radagon's union with Queen Marika.
But Rykard fed himself to the blasphemous serpent, Great Rune and all.
Helm of the golden lion, with flowing red hair. Worn by General Radahn.
Radahn inherited the furious, flaming red hair of his father Radagon, and is fond of its heroic implications.
"I was born a champion's cub. Now I am the Lord of the Battlefield's lion."
Legendary sorcery associated with the Carian queen.
Uses the caster as a vessel to incarnate a cold, dark moon, then sends it floating toward foes. The dark moon dispels all sorcery that touches it, and temporarily reduces magic damage negation for those it strikes.
This moon was encountered by a young Ranni, led by the hand of her mother, Rennala. What she beheld was cold, dark and veiled in occult mystery.

Glintstone sorcerers are the descendants of astrologers, a fact that the Carians remain of aware of. Even if their fate has been long severed from the stars.
TheCarian Royal Familywas afactioninELDEN RING(2022).
Members of the Carian Royal Family were prolific magic users and erstwhile heads of theAcademy of Raya Lucaria, who were famous for developing their own glintstone sorceries.[1]They originated from the mist-laden region in the west of theLands Between, known asLiurnia of the Lakes.
The Carian Royal Family would reach its peak underRennala, Queen of the Full Moon. In her youth, she was a prominent champion who would go on to charm the academy with her lunar magic, becoming its master. She also led the Glintstone Knights and established the house of Caria as royalty.[2]
The Carian Royals have always been closely associated with the western coast of Liurnia,[3]which is the location of their estate, theCaria Manor, as well as the Three Sisters region immediately behind it. Another location of importance was theCarian Study Hall, a large library in eastern Liurnia that connects to the region'sDivine Tower.[4]
The Carian royals were served by magic preceptors notable for large hats with the movements of the stars drawn on the inside of the brim,[5]as well as on their bright blue gowns.[6]All glintstone sorcerers are the descendants ofastrologers, a fact that the Carians remained aware of.[5]The astrologers preceded the sorcerers and had established themselves in mountaintops that nearly touched the sky, and considered the Fire Giants their neighbors.[7]They would read fate in the stars, but alas, the night sky no longer cradles fate.[8]
However, the Carian royal family were mostly known for the famousenchanted knightsthat served them. These enchanted knights, anointed by the Lunar Queen, were heroes of the highest honors,[9]and served as direct retainers to the kingdom's princesses.[10]Theirswordswere embedded with blue glintstone, and could serve as catalysts, letting them wield sorcerous battle skills. Despite numbering fewer than twenty, this power made them a match for even thechampions of goldin battle.[11]They combined this art with their swordsmanship to maintain pressure upon their foes, striking in waves of steel and sorcery.[12]The Carian knights never wavered, and even had sorceries that could alleviate the buildup of sleep or madness.[13]There were also enchanted troll knights among their number, comrades of young Rennala, bound by oath.[14]They were called into service when the Queen invoked an oath they swore. These trolls were treated as true knights of Caria, and would fight arm in arm with their human comrades.[15]
The famousLorettawas once a royal Carian knight,[16]and served as a personal guard to Carian royalty.[17]Despite fighting mounted and using awar sickle, her favored weapon was said to be the bow, and she developed sorceries imitating the power of a greatbow.[18]She would leave her service in search of a haven forAlbinaurics,[19]but anapparitionof her remains to defend Caria Manor to this day. Several Albinauric mages, such asPidia, remained as servants to the Carian Royal family,[20]seemingly facing less persecution there then in other parts of the Lands Between.
The oldest sorcery devised by the Carians would conjure anenemy-seeking glintblade, and it would serve as a prototype for more enhancedsword-phalanxsorceries wielded by royal enchanted knights.[21]They also created sorceries that would conjure magic swords that couldsweep,sliceandpiercetheir enemies. Some sorceries were said to have been taught to them by the enigmaticCrystalians, to mark the swearing of an old concord.[22]
Due to the influence of the Carians,[23]the Lazuli Conspectus would eventually developed in the Academy. The scholars of this conspectus sought to master Carian sorcery, and viewed the moon as equal to the stars.[24]This would be seen as a heterodox pursuit, or even outright heresy,[25]by their colleagues at the academy.
WhenQueen Marika the Eternalestablished her new Age of theErdtree, she dispatched a champion known asRadagonto lead her armies against the lands of Liurnia. Not much was known about Radagon before he joined the ranks in the Liurnian Wars,[26]but he was seen as a great champion with flowing red locks, and he would lead a great golden host to Liurnia, where he would meet Rennala in battle.[27]
Radagon would fight two wars against Rennala and the Academy,[28]both of which saw no clear victor.[29]Instead, Radagon eventually repented his territorial aggressions by cleansing himself withCelestial Dew,[30]swore his love to Rennala and became the husband of the Carian Queen.[31]
He married her at theChurch of Vows,[32]and it would be this matrimonial union, and reconciliation between the houses of the Erdtree and the Full Moon[33]that would eventually have grave consequences for the Carians, as it was during the age of the Erdtree, that Carian astrology withered on the vine, as the fate once writ in the night skies had been fettered by theGolden Order.[34]
Rennala would bequeath Radagon with agreatsword,[35]to honor a long standing tradition in

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Dragon Communion
Dragon Communion(竜餐,Ryūsan) is a ritual inELDEN RING(2022). It involves the hunting ofdrakes, the descendants ofAncient Dragons, and the consumption of theirgravel stone-coveredhearts.
Specifically,Dragon Communionis the act of consuming dragon hearts in order to acquire thedraconic powerswithin. The hearts are consumed at aDragon Communion Altarin the presence of a fallen dragon.
In the distant past, the lord of theancient dragons,Placidusax, was attacked by the great drake,Bayle the Dread. Their clash ended in a stalemate and left both gravely wounded, with Bayle fleeing the field of battle.[1]
As punishment for Bayle's transgression, the Ancient Dragons established the practice of Dragon Communion. One of Placidusax's followers, Florissax, took mortal form asa humanoid priestessto spread the ritual.[2]Warriors were lured to this cause with the promise of great power which could only be acquired by consuming the heart of a drake.[3][4]
As time passed, the practice would continue without influence from the priestesses; many practitioners would forget the original purpose of the hunt and would simply carry on consuming hearts in pursuit of greater power.[citation needed]Some drakes have become aware of this practice, such asEkzykes the Decaying, who even after succumbing toMalenia'srotwould never forget his hatred and thus keeps himself stationed at the entrance of theCathedral of Dragon Communion, so that he may kill or deter any would-be practitioners before they can reach the altar[5].
Dragon Communion practitioners develop a hunger for the hearts as they hunt, which gradually intensifies as they devour more hearts. This leads some to commune without restraint, causing their bodies and minds to become increasingly wyrm-like.[6]The end-result is the full transformation intoMagma Wyrms, dragon-like creatures with pitifully small wings, incapable of flight and cursed to crawl the earth on their bellies until the end of their days.[7]Ironically, this end often comes at the hands of their fellow practitioners as their own hearts become fair game for communion.

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: The Crucible
The primordial form of theErdtreeis close in nature to life itself, and thisspear, modeled on its crucible, is imbued with ancientholyessence.
TheCrucible,[5][6][7]also known as thegolden Crucible,[3]theprimordial crucible,[4]or thecrucible of life,[2]was a primordial matter that formed into theErdtree.[2]All life was once held together within the Crucible.[4]
The primordial Crucible was the divine essence that became theErdtreeand the place where all life energy was once blended together.[2][4][8]It was said to be close in nature to life itself,[9][10]and was represented by gold with a reddish tint—primordial gold, the color of homeward yearning.[11]The power of the Crucible was also held in the armor of theCrucible Knights,[12]and channeled by their weapons.[9]
The aspects of various creatures grew on the bodies of humans andgiantslong ago, such as feathers, scales, and knots. Now considered vestiges of the Crucible, their presence was considered the mark ofdivinityin ancient times.[13]Of the Crucible's gifts,[5]thehornsentconsidered the tangled horn to be the most significant sign of primacy.[14]As society advanced, they were increasingly disdained as an impurity.[15]Budding hornsandoverlapping fangsthat grew on herbivorous and carnivorousbeastswere held in the same regard.[16][17]

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Glintstone
Glintstoneis a type of mineral inELDEN RING(2022).
Sorcery draws from the power embedded in glintstone.[1]It is said that glintstone is the amber of the cosmos, and that it contains the vitality of the stars.[2]Glintstones have a wide variety of applications: they can be embedded in staffs used to cast sorceries,[3]and the stone crowns worn by followers of theAcademy of Raya Lucaria Conspectuses;[4]used as ornamentation in various weapons;[5][6][7]or used as a receptacle for a sorcerer's soul after removal using aPrimal Glintstone Blade.[8][9]In addition, many glintstone sorceries conjure projectiles made of glintstone, which can be launched at enemies.[10]
Glintstone typically has a crystalline appearance, and many varieties exist. The glintstone embedded in the staffs of theAcademy of Raya Lucaria's sorcerers is a turquoise colour,[11]a colour shared by many of the fundamental glintstone sorceries, while glintstone used by theCarian Royal Familyis typically blue.[12][13]
Red glintstone is said to be formed from the blood of sacrifices, and enhances the power of thorn sorceries.[14][15]Red glintstone is also used in the staves wielded byGelmir Man-Serpents, which can enhance the effect of lava sorceries.[16]This glintstone has an apparent connection to the blood star.[17]
Rarer forms of glintstone include dark purple crystals which can enhance gravity sorceries[18], and sullied glintstone which enhances death sorceries and is considered heretical by the academy.[19]

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Omen (Lore)
TheOmen(忌み,Imi,or 忌み子,Imigo) are accursed beings found in theLands Betweenborn without the grace of theErdtree.[1]
The Omen are hulking and brutish in appearance, covered in twisted horns growing from their body. Certain Omen, such asMorgott, the Omen KingandMohg, Lord of Bloodalso have tails and feathered wings. These traits are reminiscent of the vestiges of the Crucible, considered a signifier of the divine in ancient times, but reviled as an impurity as civilization advanced.[2]
Omen babies have all their horns excised, which causes most to perish; they are memorialized with small fetish dolls in the likeness of an infant Omen with their horns cut off.[3]Meanwhile, Omen born to royalty keep their horns, but are kept underground, unbeknownst to anyone, where they are bound by shackles for eternity.[4]Fetish dolls depicting the Omen infant with their horns left intact are crafted in secret to memorialize these Omen.[5]Wraithserupt from the bodies of Omen whose horns remain intact, and can also be expelled via the breath, or used to enwreathe their weapons.
Omen are seen as impure due to their cursed blood.[6][7]For this reason they are hunted byOmenkillers,  the first of which was the perfumerRollo, who wield giant cleavers comprised of amputated Omen horns that cause blood loss,[8]and wear masks imitating the evil spirits that haunt the Omen in their nightmares.[9]The perfumerTriciaand her associates[6]dedicated their efforts to treating Omen, among others seen as impure. When her efforts failed, she instead became their companion when they died, ensuring they could pass peacefully.[10]
Despite being reviled, excised Omen are sometimes used as soldiers. They are awarded cleavers of colossal size, taking advantage of the Omen's brute strength. However, the blades are etched with a remnant of a deteriorative malediction to ensure that the blade can be taken away.[11]They occasionally can be found wearing black cloaks, and certain Omen among these cloaked variants have taken to worshiping thePrince of Death.

Living Jarsare beings and enemies inELDEN RING(2022)that can be found across theLands Between.
Sentient, animated jars found throughout theLands Between. They are brought to life by human flesh and blood, and are considered a kindly folk[1], however they will protect themselves from perceived threats. They contain human innards within them, from which they inherit the dregs of those who came before.[2]Fragments of their bodies are sought after due to the magical power locked within, making them targets of poachers.[3]
An enclave of peaceful Living Jars reside inJarburg, on the cliffs ofLiurnia of the Lakes.

Small, childlike Living Jars, often found under the protection of Warrior Jars. They are often passive unless provoked.
Living Jars with distinct yellow lids. Their primary tactic is to rush at their enemies and then explode, killing themselves and dealing damage to friends and foes alike. They will also explode if they come into contact with fire.
Larger Living Jars that contain the remnants of warriors[4]. They pass these warrior's innards from jar to jar, carrying their dreams of greatness with them.[5]

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Walking Mausoleum | Elden Ring Wiki
Wandering Mausoleumsare specialLocationsinElden Ring. Mausoleums appear as walking buildings with four legs and are found throughout the Lands Between, often with their signature bells attached. Players must attack the skull-like deposits on the structure while avoiding damage to get the mausoleum to become accessible. These can appear on either the legs or along the base of the building, the latter of which necessitates jumping on top of it.
Hit the skull-like deposits to make the mausoleum collapse. These skulls can be either on its feet, or around the mausoleum on top.
Around Mausoleums are spectral knights roaming the arena. After bringing it down, they disappear.
Mausoleum can attack by either stomping or performing a slam attack (Non-Bell variant). Their stomp is a near guaranteed death, for invaders/enemies included. The Snowfield Mausoleum fires exploding magic projectiles in an arc around it, dealing heavy Magic damage. It's recommended to hit the Grace at theApostate Derelictto respawn in case of death.
Place yourBossRemembrance at the altar to Duplicate it. (Note: You do not have to have the Remembrance with you when you do this. If you previously acquired and used it, you can still receive a duplicate at a later time in your playthrough). Only one use per Mausoleum. Pick wisely!
It should be noted that you cannot regain a Remembrance Weapon that you have already obtained (in the same playthrough at least).
Mausoleums without a bell seem to only be able to duplicate Remembrances of bosses that aren't children of Radagon and/or Marika.(via community testing:Regal Ancestor Spirit,Astel Naturalborn of the Void,Lichdragon Fortissax,Fire Giant,Maliketh, the Black Blade,Dragonlord Placidusax,Hoarah Loux, WarriorandElden Beastare the only bosses with Remembrances that can be duplicatedanywhere. Demigods' Remembrances, likeMorgott's andMalenia's, will work with bell variant Mausoleumsonly.)
The Castle Sol and Consecrated Snowfield Mausoleums appear to be bugged for some people where using one of them renders the other unusable but this seems to not apply to everyone.
Players will hear mausoleums as they emit a distinctly loud bell sound as they walk about. They usually have a small roaming area, so they are easy to find. When you first want to access a wandering mausoleum, you must either attack the deposits on its feet or use the environment to climb up, jump onto the wandering mausoleum and destroy the deposits around the structure itself.  This can take considerable time depending on the location.
Once the mausoleum is static, you can enter it at any time to perform aRemembrance Duplication: This is only available once per mausoleum, so pick wisely! Performing this rite will enable you to obtain the multipleRemembrance Weapons (Boss Weapons)and magic that they grant. Boss Armor is not gated behind their remembrances, but you must have defeated them to purchase fromEniaat theRoundtable Hold.
There are a total of 7 Wandering Mausoleums in Elden Ring. Monuments with bells will duplicate any boss remembrance. Monumentswithoutbells will only duplicate the remembrance of a non-shard bearer boss. Each reward can only be received once per playthrough.
Weeping Peninsula, Bell: In the western area, east ofIsolated Merchant's Shack. [Map Link] During the "late night" period of the day/night cycle, the Mausoleum stops moving for approximately seven minutes of real time. It will stop wandering wherever it is when this time is reached, but quitting out and reloading will leave it standing still at its spawn position, closest to the Isolated Merchant's Shack.
Liurnia of the Lakes, Bell: northeast ofRaya Lucaria Academy, in the waters in front ofRaya Lucaria Crystal TunnelGrace [Map Link]. To access this Wandering Mausoleum you must travel west of the tunnel entrance. Then you need to use the spirit spring to jump onto the Mausoleum when it walks close enough to the cliff wall. You can experiment with the spirit spring jump and also double jump with Torrent after using the spring and take no fall damage. You can also jump from the tombstones on the northern cliff, but you risk dying if you miss. Once on top of the Mausoleum, knock off enough skull piles to subdue it. Like the Weeping Peninsula Mausoleum, it stops wandering during "late night" for seven to eight minutes. Alternatively, hitting the legs will stop the mausoleum from moving, then you can snipe enough skulls to get it to kneel using a bow. The various rocks in the area can be used to get the right angle, the skulls are all on and around the grassy area level.
Liurnia of the Lakes, No Bell:North of theRuined Labyrinth Graceor, due south of theMausoleum Compound Gracein Eastern Liurnia, north of the Church of Vows. It stops wandering for about seven minutes during "late night".
Liurnia of the Lakes, No Bell: due north of theMausoleum Compound Gracenear Uld Palace Ruins, north of theChurch of Vows[Map Link]. It stops wandering at night, in sync with #3.
Mountaintops of the Giants, Bell: Just outsideCastle Solin the northern area. It stops wandering during "late night" for seven to eight minutes. [Map Link]
Consecrated Snowfield, Bell: northwest ofOrdina, next to theApostate DerelictGrace.Warning: This one fires magical artillery into the air, bombarding the surroundings until it is subdued.It does not stop moving at night, but it will stop attacking when you're within the walls of the Apostate Derelict church, and won't start again immediately when you step outside. [Map Link]
Deeproot Depths, Bell: North of theThe Nameless Eternal CityGrace. Can be jumped upon by climbing on the roots in the area (be careful of the manyBasilisks), then you must destroy skulls on the top of the Mausoleum instead of the feet. It will stop wandering for exactly seven minutes during the "late night" period of the day/night cycle. [Map Link]
Additionally, threeRemembrance Duplication Coffinswere added in the Shadow of the Erdtree expansion which serve the same purpose.
Wandering Mausoleumsare large, mobile structures inELDEN RING(2022)which serve as means to duplicateRemembrances.
The Wandering Mausoleums are the resting places of soulless demigods who areMarika'sunwanted children.[1][2][3]They take the form of large buildings mounted atop four legs, which wander around set areas throughout theLands Between. Some Mausoleums have massive bells hanging from the undersides of their structures which can be heard from afar, ringing to constantly mourn its soulless demigods.[4]Most have skull-like formations in their feet which disappear and release a small amount ofghostflamewhen hit.
They are often guarded byMausoleum KnightsandMausoleum Soldiers, who beheaded themselves in order to follow their masters into death,[5]a self-inflicted curse that ties their spirits to the land.[6]Their armor depicts the mausoleum bell,[7]and the knights don wing-shaped ornamentations that evoke theDeathbirds.[8]
The shields of the Mausoleum Knights is emblazoned with the eclipsed sun, which is a symbol of the Mausoleums.[9]The eclipse is the protective star of the soulless demigods and aids the Mausoleum Knights in keeping Destined Death at bay.[10]
To use mausoleums and do the process of Remembrance duplication, the player needs to enter a Wandering Mausoleum and interact with the headless corpse on the altar inside. Duplication can only be performed once per mausoleum. Remembrances belonging toShardbearersmay only be duplicated at Wandering Mausoleums with bells, while all other Remembrances can be duplicated at any Wandering Mausoleum (as shown on the table below). Remembrances can be duplicated even after they have already been used.
Typically, access to Wandering Mausoleums is granted by hitting the white skull-shaped forms found on the structure's feet, causing the Mausoleum to lower itself to a height where the player can climb onto them. In most cases,Mausoleum Knights,Mausoleum Soldiers, andMausoleum Footsoldierswill spawn near the Wandering Mausoleums, serving as an additional obstacle to the player's access to the structures.
