area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Golden Order Fundamentalism | Elden Ring Wiki
Golden Order Fundamentalismis a strict religious practice inElden Ring. It holds the Elden Ring andQueen Marika'srule as perfect and absolute. Any perceived imperfections or threats to the Golden Order are subsequently wiped out or excluded by its members. Even the act of accusing the Golden Order of being flawed is deemed heretical. SeeGolden Order Incantationsfor the related spell class.
Following only the guidance of the great Elden Ring." - D, Hunter of the Dead
Golden Order Fundamentalism began withRadagon of the Golden Orderas he studied sorceries during his time as husband toRennala, Queen of the Full Moon, and later studied incantations as the Lord consort to Queen Marika. He became adept at both, as fundamentalism is considered scholarship in all but name. Golden Order Fundamentalism is unique in that it infuses both intelligence and faith for its incantations and sacred seal. The practice is predicated on two primary concepts, the law of regression and the law of causality. Regression is described as the pull of meaning; that all things yearn eternally to converge. While causality is the pull between meanings; that which links all things in a chain of relation. This language is similar toMiriel, Pastor of Vowsdialogue when given any prayerbook; "Oh, what have we here? Very well, let us both learn together. Heresy is not native to the world; it is but a contrivance. All things can be conjoined". Miriel speaks with familiarity about Radagon, and knows far more about him than most characters. It could be inferred that the two knew each other during Radagon's time at Rennala's side studying sorceries, and when Radagon later cleansed himself at theChurch of Vowswithcelestial dew. However, Golden Order Fundamentalism is not as accepting as Miriel is, and incantations were created for hunters to cleanseThose Who Live in Death.
Seen as a pox to the Golden Order, Those Who Live in Death are the result of spirits returning to life as undead rather than to theErdtree. Deemed abhorrent by those of the Golden Order, fundamentalists hunted them down without mercy.D, Hunter of the Dead, andD, Beholder of Deathwere among those who held Those Who Live in Death in contempt. The two known as D were inseparable, and found solace in the Golden Order, as it was the only institution not to revile them as accursed beings. As such they followed the tenets to the point of fanaticism. But the ever brilliantGoldmasklamented what had become of the hunters according to theOrder Healingdescription, how easy it is for learning and learnedness to be reduced to the ravings of fanatics; all the good and the great wanted, in their foolishness, was an absolute evil to contend with. Does such a notion exist in the fundamentals of Order? Goldmask was a staunch believer in Golden Order Fundamentalism, but was not beneath pointing out its flaws and trying to uncover a solution. At the end of his pursuit he envisioned aring, a blazing golden halo symbolizing the perfection of order. He was not the only one to be unsatisfied with the Golden Order's teachings. The youngEmpyreanMiquellawas a gifted prodigy who learned Golden Order Fundamentalism and gifted his father with offensive spells that were made of rings of light. He however could not grant his half-brotherGodwyna true death nor cure his twin sisterMaleniaof herscarlet rot, and so abandoned fundamentalism and instead invested his knowledge in unalloyed gold.

A mask designed to resemble a blazing golden halo. Created and left behind by Lord Goldmask, a staunch pursuer of Golden Order fundamentalism. Strenthens Golden Order incantations.Its striking design represents both the brilliant inspiration that once shone upon him, and the vision of a ring that he will surely find at the end of his pursuit."To you who seek to shine as I do, wear it well!"
A sword made to commemorate the death of Godwyn the Golden, first of the demigods to die.
Infused with the humble prayer of a young boy; "O brother, lord brother, please die a true death."
Rune discovered by the noble Goldmask.Used to restore the fractured Elden Ring when brandished by the Elden Lord.
A rune of transcendental ideology which will attempt to perfect the Golden Order.
The current imperfection of the Golden Order, or instability of ideology, can be blamed upon the fickleness of the gods no better than men. That is the fly in the ointment.
TheGolden Order(黄金律,Ōgonritsu) is a philosophical and theological movement inELDEN RING(2022). It refers to the removal of theRune of Deathfrom theElden Ringand the historic reign ofQueen Marika the Eternal. Its greatest symbols are theErdtreeand theGrace of Gold. It is the dominant set of beliefs in theLands Between.
The Golden Order was established by Queen Marika followingMaliketh's triumph over theGloam-Eyed Queenand herGodskin Apostles.[1][2]She extracted the Rune of Death from the Elden Ring and sealed it inside hershadowbound beast.[3][4][5]In doing so, she suppressed the power of herEmpyreanrival and granted immortality to herself and herdemigodoffspring, theGolden Lineage.[6][7]
The Golden Order was a governing principle, a religion, and a philosophy. It was founded on the principle that Marika was the one true god,[8]and was propagated by theTwo Fingers.[9]It replaced the concept ofDestined Deathwith that ofErdtree Burial.
The Golden Order was capable of integrating conflicting ideologies and practices. Thedragon cultof theroyal capitalwas compatible because theancient dragons'lightningwas imbued with gold.[10]Later, theErdtreefaith absorbed the practice ofglintstone sorcery.[11]Concepts that threatened to shatter the Order entirely, such aslife in death, were labeled as heresy and violently persecuted by the Golden Order.[12]
Golden Order Fundamentalism was a scholarly pursuit that combined both intelligence and faith.[13]It attempted to interpret the fundamentals of the Golden Order.[14]Fundamentalism was based on two concepts: theLaw of Regression, the pull of meaning and the yearning to converge;[15]and theLaw of Causality, the pull between meanings which links all things in a chain of relation.[16]
Among the Golden Order Fundamentalists were the hunters ofThose Who Live in Death, who abandoned learning in search of an absolute evil to contend with.[17]Miquella, who once created Fundamentalist incantations to give to his fatherRadagon, abandoned Fundamentalism as it could not treatMalenia's rot.[18]Other notable followers of Golden Order Fundamentalism includedBrother Corhyn,Goldmask, and the twinsD. Hunter of the DeadandD, Beholder of Death.

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Endings
The fallen leaves tell a story. Of how a Tarnished became Elden Lord.
ELDEN RING(2022)features six total endings: Age of Fracture, Age of Order, Age of the Duskborn, Blessing of Despair, Age of the Stars and the Lord of Frenzied Flame.
The Age of Fracture is the simplest to obtain, only requiringThe Tarnishedto finish the game, while all others demand completion their respective side quests beforehand. The Age of Fracture, Age of Order, Age of the Duskborn and Blessing of Despair endings see The Tarnished rise as Marika's new Elden Lord of theGolden Order, mending the Elden Ring, and ushering in their new Age of choice to rule over. The Age of the Stars ending sees The Tarnished aidRanni the Witchin oustingMarikaand remaining at her side as Ranni's first Elden Lord. The Lord of Frenzied Flame ending, caused by the possession of the Frenzied Flame, overrides the possibility of any other ending. The Tarnished's disregards the notion of becoming Elden Lord becoming the Lord of Frenzied Flame instead and incinerating everything that came before.
For The Tarnished to separate themselves from the Frenzied Flame's influence after being inherited, they must aquireMiquella's Needleand follow its specific conditions of use. Once the Frenzied Flame is ridded, it can not be reclaimed in any way, preventing the Lord of Frenzied Flame ending.
The Tarnished becomes Elden Lord, fulfilling theTwo Fingers'splans of using the Tarnished to restore the sense of stability not felt since the Elden Ring was shattered. TheGolden Orderremains in the truest state possible to what it once was and the status quo is restored.
The Tarnished becomes Elden Lord, fulfilling Goldmask's idea of a "Perfect" Golden Order, based upon his research into how it had fallen to its current state. Having realized that the imperfections of the Golden Order stemmed from the fickleness of the gods, who in fact were no better than men, Goldmask's new transcendental ideology attempts to bring true order to theLands Between.
The Tarnished becomes Elden Lord, wielding theruneborn fromFiaand thePrince of Death'sunion. Just as theGolden Orderhad been created by confiningDestined Death, the Tarnished creates a new order of death restored. The principle of life in death is embeded within this order, andThose Who Live in Deathare allowed to live in peace.
The Tarnished becomes Elden Lord, fulfilling the Dung Eater's twisted vision of a cursed world. All will become cursed, thus none can be scorned, which despite its radicalism, does bring order back to theLands Between.
The Tarnished helps Ranni fulfil her vision of a Lands Between without the Golden Order by allowing her to replaceMarikain godhood and taking the role of her consort. Ranni ushers in a new order not of gold, but of the stars and moon of the chill night. Rather than make herself and her order objects of worship, she chooses instead to keep her order and theLands Betweenat a great divide, removing the certainties that had existed during Marika's rule.
The Tarnished and Ranni leave the Lands Between, embarking on a thousand year voyage into darkness under the wisdom of the Moon.
Rather than become Elden Lord, The Tarnished becomes the Lord of Frenzied Flame, fulfilling the machinations ofShabriri, and theThree Fingers'swill. The Tarnished is left almost completely alone, the Frenzied Flame rapidly consuming everything in existence.
IfMelinawas not sacrificed, she is seen vowing to hunt down and kill the Tarnished for not heeding her earlier warnings.
After thefinal bossis slain, they will return alone to a room with Marika's statue and a Grace. Ranni's summon sign will also appear on the ground close by to the Marika's statue, if Ranni's questline has been completed. The Tarnished will now have the option to choose their ending by interacting with Marika's statue, or, if present, Ranni's summon sign. If The Tarnished possesses the Frenzied Flame, Ranni's summon sign will not appear unless the Frenzied Flame is ridden byMiquella's Needle. In this case, the only option will be to interact with Marika's statue, and the Lord of Frenzied Flame ending will automatically begin, offering no alternative choice at all.
Interacting with Marika's statue without the Frenzied Flame will allow The Tarnished to choose from one of three possible mending runes to repair the Elden Ring that can obtained during their adventures. Once the respective rune has been chosen, the Age of Order, Age of the Duskborn, or Blessing of Despair ending will begin. A fourth option to "Mend the Elden Ring" without a rune is always available, and if chosen, results in the Age of Fracture ending.
If present, interacting with the Ranni's summon sign, instead of Marika's statue, will begin the Age of the Stars ending.
In all cases, the nearby Grace can be used to teleport anywhere else and return later, allowing the ending to be postponed and play to continue.

TheFingerprint Stone Shieldis ashieldfound inELDEN RING(2022).
A great stone shield with an intricately carved fingerprint design. One of the heaviest of all greatshields.

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Caria Manor
Caria Manoris a dungeon inELDEN RING(2022).
A large estate in the north-west of Liurnia. The manor was once the home of theCarian Royal Family[1], who ruled over Liurnia and governed theAcademy of Raya Lucaria.[2]After the Academy turned on the Carians, the Cuckoo Knights launched an assault on the manor, catching the Carian Knights off guard. However, the Cuckoos were caught in a magic snare which keeps their souls trapped within the manor.[3]
In recent times, there have been rumours of vassals of the royal family gathering in the manor's grounds, possibly including the secretiveRanni the Witch.[4]

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Crumbling Farum Azula
Crumbling Farum Azulais a region and legacy dungeon inELDEN RING(2022)accessed from theMountaintops of the Giantsafter burning the Erdtree.
A giant ruined temple city in the sky, located above the sea to the east of theLands Between. Once a royal city and the seat of theDragonlord Placidusax, Farum Azula has been crumbling since time immemorial.[1]Now, it is a mausoleum, guarded by chosenBeastmenwho wield weapons clad in lightning.[2]The storm beyond time rages in the center of the crumbling city, and at its heart is the Dragonlord's seat, where he awaits the return of his god.[3]
As well as Beastmen, Farum Azula is home to a number ofAncient Dragonswho roost on the floating fragments of the city. There is a small population ofWormfacesdwelling in one of the lower levels of the city. It appears thatDeathroothas spread throughout parts of the city as well. The great rotundum at the center of Farum Azula is the dwelling place ofMaliketh, the Black Blade, the protector of theRune of Death.[4]
It is here that theTarnishedfinds themselves after they set theErdtreeaflame, and where they finally unbind the Rune of Death, releasing it upon the Lands Between.
Farum Azula can only be accessed in full after setting the Erdtree aflame at theForge of the Giants. After doing so, the Tarnished will wake up on a bridge leading to the city. The area can also be previewed by taking one of theSending Gates(labeled"Crumbling Lands") at theFour BelfriesinLiurnia. This Sending Gate leads to an isolated floating fragment of stone from which the rest of Farum Azula can be seen but not accessed.
The only area in the Lands Between from which Farum Azula is visible is theIsolated Divine Tower.

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Volcano Manor
Volcano Manoris a legacy dungeon located onMt. Gelmir.
The Volcano Manor is home to therecusantsofPraetor Rykard, fierce warriors who wage war against theErdtreeand theRoundtable. The recusants are led by Rykard's consort,Lady Tanith. PowerfulTarnishedare extended invitations to join the Volcano Manor and are given contracts to hunt other Tarnished in service of the Roundtable. Tarnished who prove themselves are offered an audience with Praetor Rykard himself, which will inevitably end with the serpentinedemigoddevouring them, making them forever a part of his "family".
The Volcano Manor is besieged by the forces ofthe Royal Capital.
The Volcano Manor is one of the game's most complex locations. It can be reached in multiple ways and you can progress through from different directions.
The fastest, but most gimmicky way to reach it is by letting theAbductor Virginat the bottom of the Raya Lucaria Academy grapple you to death. You will still drop your runes, but be respawned right within the Volcano Manor area. From here there are two paths that are each a point of no return. One leading to the rest of the manor, the other brings you to theAbductor Virginduo bossfight and back to theAltus Plateau. For the Abductor Virgin boss, search for the cave with multiple drop-down platforms. To progress deeper into the manor, jump down the lava waterfall. If you die here before reaching a grace, you will be respawned where the Abductor Virgin dropped you within Volcano Manor. From here you can explore the area, defeat theGodskin Nobleand either make it back to the manor entrance withLady Tanithand the other npcs, or skip their quests and head straight to the gateway portal leading toPraetor Rykard.
The regular paths to enter the manor are either on foot/horseback acrossMt. Gelmir, or to be teleported right to the Volcano Manor entrance grace byRyaonce reaching theAltus Plateau. You won't be able to reach the bosses or explore the rest of the area from here unless you accept Lady Tanith's offer to get theDrawing-Room Key. If you join the manor, a list of NPCs become available there:Bernahl,Patches,Rya,Diallos Hoslow. To get all the content out of the manor, you have to wait with fighting Rykard until reaching theMountaintops of the Giants, so that you can do all of the following NPC invasions for the manor:Old Knight Istvan, Rileigh the Idle,Great Horned Tragoth, Vargram the Raging Wolf + Errant Sorcerer Wilhelm,Juno Hoslow, Knight of Blood. After defeating Juno Hoslow,Tanithoffers to send you to Rykard, where you can then start the boss fight. Remember to completeRya's quest before defeatingJuno Hoslow, Knight of Blood, otherwise you'll be locked out ofTanith's dialogue regarding Rya.

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Liurnia of the Lakes
The majority of Liurnia, known for its vast forests and ever-present fog, is sinking into a lake.
Liurnia of the Lakesis a region in theLands Between.
The westernmost region of the Lands Between. Characterized by its boggy woodlands, sheer cliffs, and pervasive mists, much of the region is sinking into the Liurnia Lake.
On the eastern side of the region, the Liurnia Highway runs north to south, connecting the land to theAltus PlateauandLimgrave. The western coast is closely associated with the royal family of Caria, as it is the location of their stronghold inCaria Manor. TheAcademy of Raya Lucariarises above the lake in the center of Liurnia at a junction between two highroads, with theAcademy Gate Townsprawling around its base as the buildings slowly sink into the waters.
Liurnia is mostly under the control of Raya Lucaria and itsKnights of the Cuckoo. TheCariansalso maintain a presence at their manor and theCarian Study Hall. The Lunar QueenRennalawas master of the academy, but she is now locked in its grand library.[1][2]
In theFounding Rain of Stars,glintstonerained upon the land.[3][4]The founding glintstone sorcerers[5][6]AzurandLusat- both of whom had seen into the abyss from which the rain came[7][8]- founded the most venerableConspectusesat the Academy of Raya Lucaria.[9]The Academy itself was built on a massive glintstone deposit visible from below in theLake of Rot, and the entire region of Liurnia is scattered with glintstone crystals. The mineral has since become central to the identity of the region.
Rennala, once a young astrologer, walked with her eyes fixed on the night sky.[10]Though she had been infatuated with the stars, she encountered an enchantingFull Moon.[11]The bewitching power of her moon eventually propelled her to her mastery of Raya Lucaria. She also came to lead the Glintstone Knights and established the House of Caria.[12]In this role she anointed the Carian Knights and her house bestowed upon them Carian glintstone sorceries.[13][14]Her younger sisterRellanalearned glintstone sorcery fromCount Ymirbefore he turned away from his faith to the moon; Rellana and Rennala also discovered theTwin Moons, and the former learned to use incarnations of them.[15][16]
The grand estate ofCaria Manorwas home to the Carian Royal Family.[17]On the upper level of the manor there are the Royal Moongazing Grounds, which may have at one point allowed the Carians to gaze on the enchanting lunar body.
The championLord Radagonof the Erdtree worshipers harbored territorial aggression, and his neighbors to the west came under attack in the First and Second Wars of Liurnia.[18]Radagon was at the head of these armies, and his glory was said to have been burning red.[19][20]However, the Enchanted Knights were well-trained and were a match even for the Erdtree's champions of gold.[21]Both wars were ultimately unsuccessful, and neither side claimed victory in the second war.[22]

area: Liurnia of the Lakes
chapter: 4
name: Ranni's Appearance & Color Lore
Lunar Princess Ranni's iconic blue color palette is directly tied to her rejection of the Greater Will. Having slain her original demigod flesh (which possessed the red hair of her father, Radagon), her spirit now inhabits an artificial, four-armed doll body.
This vessel's distinctive pale-blue skin, snow-white traveling clothes, and pointed hat were meticulously modeled after her secret childhood mentor, the Snow Witch (Renna). Because the Snow Witch was a master of cold, frost, and lunar sorceries, the doll's design reflects those icy elements. Furthermore, the translucent blue spirit face hovering to the side of the doll's head represents Ranni's literal soul, which manifests in the deep blue hue universally associated with Carian royalty and primeval glintstone magic.

name: Ranni the Witch
area: Liurnia of the Lakes
---
Ranni inhabits a doll-like body with pale blue skin. This is because she abandoned
her original Empyrean body on the Night of the Black Knives, transferring her soul
into a small snow witch puppet to escape the fate imposed on her by the Two Fingers.
Her blue colouration reflects her connection to the moon and cold sorceries of
Nokstella.
